# Pass 3 — Domain catalogue (draft)

Draft catalogue of domain-cluster modules and Pass-3-level observations, accumulated during the Pass 1 walk. **Not fully curated** — agent filled large sections itself with variable quality; manual curation required
before Pass 6 emission.

Sources:
- `pass-1-classification-review.md` — `.csproj`-level classification + Naming caveats
- `folder-tree.md` — annotated folder tree with module tags
- This file — file-level dispersal, module assignments, detailed notes (curation pending)

## Known concerns before use
- **All `game-*` module boundaries are tentative** (see Naming caveats in `pass-1-classification-review.md`)
- Some sections user-curated (early blocks) vs agent-generated in bulk (later) — quality variable
- Each module will be validated file-by-file during Pass 3

---

## Cross-cutting infrastructure detail (from Section E)

### ObjectModel — dispersal profile

**518 files, ~68.8k LOC across 35 subfolders.** Mirrors `SharedLib\` + `Sql.Interface\` decomposition. Dispersed across ~40 domain modules.

Largest hubs:
- `Mission\` — 162 files, ~23.6k LOC (~27% of ObjectModel)
- `Inventory\` — 118 files, ~12.1k LOC; includes massive monolith `Inventory\TerminalTackle\RodTemplates.cs` (~31k LOC)
- `Hint\` — 26 files, ~4.6k LOC
- `Tournaments\` — 39 files, ~4.3k LOC

No new module candidates emerged from inventory walk. File-level mapping in `folder-tree.md`.

### Photon.Interfaces — dispersal profile

**62 files, ~1.6k LOC** across 18 subfolders + 10 root-level files. Enum-heavy: OperationCode / ParameterCode / ErrorCode / SubOperationCode / EventCode patterns.

Root-level files of note:
- Master `OperationCode.cs` (~195 LOC, ~50 ops)
- Cross-cutting `Chat.cs` (~405 LOC) — ChatGlobals + MessageLifetime + ChatRequests + StaticChatChannels + ChatChannelNamingUtils + ChatCommands. Shared by clubs / tournaments / friendship / UGC / FT / bans / gifts / buoys / missions / leaderboards.
- `SharedConsts.cs` — protocol v1124 + 14 languages + 8 platforms + A/B test IDs + pond constants + time boundaries.

Largest subfolder: `Tournaments\` (~444 LOC).

**Misplaced folder:** `SharedMethods\` holds `InGameTimeHelper` + `TimeRewinder` utility helpers (namespace `SharedLib.Game`) — not RPC contracts; relocation candidate.

---

## Active tools detail (from Section H.1)

### DataChangesImport → `data-pipeline` module
~236 LOC, 4 files. Console .exe; imports pending DB schema-update changelog rows via interactive confirm-then-apply UPDATE statements. Invocation `DataChangesImport.exe changeTableName [-q]`. Uses `DalFactory` with `AppParametersProvider`.
**Gotchas:** interactive `Console.ReadLine()` with no timeout; silent-swallow in quiet mode.

### DataPump → `data-pipeline` module
~1.6k LOC, 6 files + nested `DataPump/DataPump/` layout. Console .exe for bulk DB-to-DB sync via MERGE; supports replication + forced-sync + cache-refresh signaling + comparison. Invocation `DataPump.exe source target table_list [q|r|f|c|e]`.
**Hardcoded forbidden-tables list** L28-32 (Users / Profiles / Transactions / Tournaments) — prevents accidental clobber, but maintainer burden grows.
Sync-over-async `.Result` L310-319. No transaction-scope grouping.

### EnvironmentSwitcher → `deploy-ops` module
~604 LOC, 11 files. WPF desktop app (`MainWindow.xaml` + MVVM); switches Windows env vars (`SvnServer` / `SvnClient`) via `Environment.SetEnvironmentVariable(..., User)`. Zero DAL / service deps. Requires UAC write. Used for local dev workflow.

### ImageDumper → `shop` / `product-delivery` (asset tooling)
~203 LOC, 4 files + ~37 MB on-disk binary. Console .exe; exports product images from DB blob storage to disk via SHA256-hash-compare + optional orphan delete. Invocation `ImageDumper.exe "output_path" [id_list]` (range syntax `1,3-5,10`).

### MaintenanceManager → `deploy-ops` module
~360 LOC, 8 files. Console .exe with Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection; generates maintenance-window JSON + uploads via SFTP (Renci.SshNet) to trigger remote deployment scripts. Args `env=<name> [message=<msg>] [type=Off|Scheduled|Custom] [endTime=<ISO8601> | duration=<TimeSpan>]`. Uses `DT.Helper.UtcNow` consistently.
**Fire-and-forget SFTP upload — no server-side write verification.**

### PerfCounterManager → `counter-publisher` (tooling)
~308 LOC, 7 files. Console .exe wrapping Windows Performance Counter API; `-i` install + `-u` uninstall. Static dispatcher to ChatServerCounters / ClubServerCounters / CommonServerCounters.
**Typo:** "Couters" in console output (twice, L64 / L73).

### PhotonConsole (under PhotonHelper) → `qa-load-testing` module
~1.4k LOC, 7 files. Console .exe; embeds Photon game-client library (`StandaloneClient`); QA / load-test tool creating N dev-account connections to a pond + simulating fishing actions. Invocation `mc|mpc|mcc count pondId maxPlayers [tournamentId] [clubId]` / `ml|mpl|mlc` / `rc` / `c` / `p <password>`.
**Single-threaded message loop + `Thread.Sleep(200ms)` throttle L126-132.** Commented-out multi-threaded refactor L211-212. Magic GUID for inventory item L214 (no explanation). User-flagged "needs heavy rewrite" — confirmed: no protocol abstraction, tight coupling, no graceful shutdown.

### ReleaseTool → `release-tooling` module (largest tool)
~15.8k LOC, 44 files, 2.3 MB. Console .exe `-<command> [args...]` with **102-case switch dispatcher** for release-time migrations. `async Task Main` but entry not awaited (L38).

17 subfolders grouped by domain:
- `Profile\` — ~7.9k LOC (largest); **4 TODOs "Replace for PS"** L777 / L782 / L828 / L830 (incomplete PlayStation migration)
- `Inventory\` — ~2.4k LOC
- `Common\` — ~784 LOC (shared helpers)
- `Money\`, `Products\` (last modified Mar 17 2024), `Releveling\`, `Tournaments\`, `LicenseUpdate\`, `Converters\`, `Messages\`, `Achievements\`, `Leagues\`, `Disconnect\`, `UserGenerator\`
- `Helpers\` — stub `SteamTranHelper`
- `Scripts\ServerVisitorsFinder\`, `Cmd\` (empty), +1 more

**~30-40 of 102 commands are pre-2020 release hotfixes** (e.g. `-r201603*`, `-r201701*`, `-fixff10`, `-fix20160915`) — candidates for archival.

### SqlCheck → `deploy-database` module
~673 LOC, 7 files. Console .exe scanning `SQL\Patches\` for `.sql` files, checking against DB `AppliedPatches` table, optionally executing pending patches with confirmation + validation (patch name must appear 2× in file as safety check). Args `env [e|q|i|m|s|f|a|p<prefix>|m=DbName|s=DbName]`.
**Sync-over-async `.Result` L319.** Patch-name-in-file check via string-replace count L147 — fragile on regex-unsafe names.

### XBoxCertChecker → `deploy-ops` / cert-management
~280 LOC, 4 files. Console .exe inspecting local X.509 certificate store for Fishing Planet + Business Partner certs with color-coded expiration reporting. **Hardcoded domain list** L14-18. **`DateTime.Now` vs cert `NotAfter` (UTC)** — timezone-drift bug L86. Copy-paste comment re-using logic from `RemoteCertificateSource`.

### PhotonTool (also under PhotonHelper)
Console client connecting to master / game / chat; debug functionality. User-noted "needs heavy rewrite".

### MaintenanceManager invocation cheat sheet
(repeated here for completeness — see above.)

## H.3 → confirmed-alive tools

### JsonVerificator (active, was H.3)
Compiled `.exe` ~73 LOC. Validates JSON deserialization against ObjectModel types via reflection. Usage `JsonVerificator.exe <file.TypeName>`. No DB access, ObjectModel-only references. Referenced from WebAdmin code.

### ProfileUtils (active, was H.3)
Compiled `.exe` ~182 LOC. Profile JSON DB ↔ file export / import. Usage `ProfileUtils.exe [in|out] <userId> <file>`. Referenced from WebAdmin code. Direct `SqlConnection` via `ConfigurationManager.ConnectionStrings["sql"]`; reflection-based SQL parameter binding; no transaction on UPDATE; silent catches. (Security: see private audit.)

---

## WebService detail (from Section I)

`WebAdmin\WebService\` — confirmed-abandoned tournament-results Web API, ~60 LOC. `CatchDataController` + Catch / Pond / Bait / Fish / Language models. Minimal error handling. Manual DateTime parsing with format `yyyyMMddTHHmm`. (Security: see private audit for auth-gap details.)

---

## SqlServerProject detail (from Section J)

`Dal\SqlServerProject\SqlServerProject.sqlproj` — **NOT a T-SQL schema project** (misleading name). **Alive and in use** — CLR-assembly: 2 `.cs` files providing:
- 3 regex UDFs: `RegexReplace`, `RegexReplaceGroup`, `RegexIsMatch`
- 1 aggregate: `StringAggDistinct`

Deployed via `CREATE ASSEMBLY` to SQL Server, consumed by `Dal\Sql.MsSql\` queries at DB level. Authoritative schema source is `SQL\Patches\`, not here. No `.refactorlog` / `.dacpac` history.

---

## Test project detail (from Section K)

### Sql.MsSql.Tests
**INTEGRATION** tests against local SQL Server `Data Source=.;Initial Catalog=Main`. 18 test files across 5 subfolders: `Async\`, `Chat\`, `Common\`, `Together\`, `Utils\`. `Utils\SqlDirectAccessProvider.cs` exposes internal `Execute*()` for raw DB ops. **9 `[Ignore]`d tests** (Converter×3, Generator×5, OfflineMessagePersister, Monetization, Tournament, Tops) + 1 commented-out test in `Generator.cs` L25-27. Uses AutoFixture for data generation. (Security: see private audit for test-config secrets.)

### NoSql.Mongo.Tests
**INTEGRATION** tests against real MongoDB at `localhost/main` (hardcoded in App.config). 4 files:
- `OnlineCashTest` — session login / validate / logout + single-session enforcement
- `ChatTest` — message save / retrieve + channel filtering
- `DiagTest` — CPU / locale / IP reporting
- `LocalTimeProvider` — mock-time test helper

### Dal.Common.Tests
Pure **UNIT** tests. 3 files:
- `CryptoTest` — AES encrypt / decrypt + salt validation
- `TraceTests` — operation-trace aggregation + filtering + formatting
- `FloatingPointPrecisionTests` — entire class decorated `[Ignore]`

### BiteSystem.Tests
**UNIT** tests, ~1.4k LOC across 8 files; **0 `[Ignore]`d**. High-quality coverage:
- `EdgeDistributionTests` — ~231 LOC, 22 methods — strategy math validation (range / monotonicity / boundary conditions / steepness ordering)
- `FishWeightGeneratorTests` — ~150 LOC — full pipeline Unrestricted vs HardCeiling, scope filtering, crossover detection, form-specific edge flags
- `FishWeightRoundingTests` — rounding mode consistency
- `FishWeightSimulationServiceTests` — ~60 LOC — bucket distribution + crossover counting
- `Common\ObjectModel\` — `ChumTests`, `FormatTests`, `HeightMapTests`, `PondsTests` (serialization + geometry parsing)

### ObjectModel.Tests
**UNIT** tests, ~18k LOC across 15 files. DTO-schema validation + logic methods; no integration / DB coverage; strong on DTO invariants, weak on API-boundary testing.

Structure:
- `Core\` — 5 files, ~6.3k LOC helpers: `RodTemplatePrototype` + `AssertInventory` + `TestFlow` + `TestCounter`. **Method names with 26-32 underscores** used as test-flow separators — intentional but confusing.
- `Fortune\` — 1 file, ~4.7k LOC `ReelOfFortuneLogicTests` (spin logic)
- `Mission\ConditionsGame\` — 1 file, ~1.8k LOC
- `DailyMissions\` — 2 files, ~1.1k LOC
- `Stats\` — 3 files, ~2k LOC (PlayerStats aggregation)
- `Travel\` — 1 file, ~0.8k LOC (travel cost + pond unlock)
- `Radar\`, `Buoys\` — 1 file each
- `App_Data\DailyMissions\CatchFishTasks\` — fixture data

### ReleaseTool.Tests
Test project for ReleaseTool. Has `TestData\` fixture folder. Not individually reviewed.


## Domain modules catalogue

- `async-processor` — async job runner Windows Service (`FP.AsyncProcessor`), one instance per platform; 47 active jobs (~40 root-level + ~42 jobs in 12 domain subfolders); scheduler loop 10s with `AbstractJob` base + `ScheduleExecutor`; CLI runners `-tt` (test tournament) / `-gw` (generate weather) / `-rw` (randomize weather) etc.
  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Async\` (~8 files ~178 LOC — `IAsyncProvider` contract: `PersistFishCatch` / `TransferTopsToWeb` / `CalculateRetentionStats` / `CaptureCcu` / `CalculatePayerStats`; DTOs `CcuDto` / `TranslationDto` / `TopFishTempDto`; `FarmRebootDto` + `FarmRebootScheduleDto` disperse to `farm-reboots`)
  - `Dal\Sql.MsSql\Async\SqlAsyncProvider.cs` (~1.4k LOC impl; 52 SqlCommand; sprocs `PersistFishCatch` / `CalculateTopTournamentPlayer`; TOP 1 farm-reboot queries)
  - `AsyncProcessor\Async.Common\` (**core infra shared by all 3 async Windows services**): `AbstractJob.cs` (~85 LOC — `JobType` enum TimeOutJob/ScheduledJob + **`JobFrequancy` TYPO** enum Hourly/Daily/Weekly/Monthly + `IsRunning` lock + `Execute()` wraps `DoExecute()`); **`ScheduleExecutor.cs` (~179 LOC — 10s scheduler loop + `Thread.Sleep` L69 + `DalFactory.GetAsyncProvider().HasSkipForToday()` L146** + **silent-swallow catch L149-151** returns false on DB error; **`DateTime.Now` vs `UtcNow` mixed** L85/L93/L109/L114 — timezone-drift risk on DST); `LogUtils.cs` minimal
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\EntryPoint.cs` (~582 LOC — Windows Service installer `FP.AsyncProcessor` + `-i`/`-u` install/uninstall + CLI job runners + 14 cache initializers L484-505 + hardwired deps `DalFactory` / `PhotonHelper` / `ClubHelper` / `EmailSender`)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\DependencyInjection.cs` (lazy-loaded ServiceProvider) + `AsyncService.cs` + `AsyncService.Designer.cs` (ServiceBase wrapper)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\Extensions\EqualityComparer.cs` (dedup util for `ReportedAbusersBanJob`)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\Scheduler\AsyncProcessorScheduleExecutor.cs` (~167 LOC — registers 47 active jobs; platform-conditional (PlayStation/Steam/Android); **4 commented-out jobs L43,77-79** — `TopWebTransferJob` dead + 3 stat-jobs embedded inside `UserCountriesCalcJob`)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\UserCountriesCalcJob.cs` (root; Daily 5:30am; **embeds `CcuStatUpdateJob` + `SalesStatUpdateJob` + `RegsStatUpdateJob` logic** internally — circular coupling with commented-out scheduler registrations L77-79; single job with 3 disguised concerns)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\CleanupCacheRefreshRequestsJob.cs` (root; Hourly xx:10 — distributed-cache maintenance; **NEW module candidate `cache-infra`** or fold into `cache`)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\CleanupServerErrorsJob.cs` + `LogClearingJob.cs` + `PingSpikesClearingJob.cs` + `ScreensClearingJob.cs` (root; daily log/error cleanup — observability housekeeping; **NEW module candidate `sys-admin`** or fold into `error-stats`)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\WeatherGenerationJob.cs` + `WeatherRandomizationJob.cs` (root; daily 11pm / 12:30am — see `weather` module)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\RemoveMessageHistoryJob.cs` (root; Daily 9pm — Chat message-history purge; **no domain subfolder** — belongs in `chat-server` / `messaging`)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\AccountClosureJob.cs` (root; TimeOut 24h — GDPR account-closure lifecycle; see `account-lifecycle`)
- `async-translator` — translation sync tool (DB ↔ SmartCat.ai external translation platform); standalone Windows Service; 4 jobs; SmartCat-based bidirectional sync
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncTranslator\Jobs\TranslationExportJob.cs` (Daily 23:00 — DB → SmartCat files) + `TranslationImportJob.cs` (SmartCat files → DB) + `TranslationSyncJob.cs` (orchestrator) + `DocumentExportJob.cs` (document-metadata export)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncTranslator\Helpers\SmartCatHelper.cs` (~178 LOC — static HttpClient with BasicAuth from `apiUser`/`apiPassword` **in `config.xml` plaintext** — no vault; AppSettings-driven endpoints `GetAccount` / `GetProjectList` / `GetProjectById` / `GetDocumentById`; polling with hardcoded `Thread.Sleep(1000)` 1s retry; **`.Result` sync-over-async** L84-86/91/98 — deadlock risk)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncTranslator\Helpers\WebClientHelper.cs` (additional HTTP utilities)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncTranslator\SmartCatModels\` (~7 API response DTOs — `ProjectInfo` / `ProjectWorkflowStage` / `DocumentInfo` / `DocumentWorkflowStage` / `DocumentExecutive` / `Task` + support)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncTranslator\Models\` (~2 internal DTOs)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncTranslator\Scheduler\` (job-scheduling init)
- ~~`async-farm-manager`~~ — **RESOLVED**: absorbed into `farm-reboots`. `AsyncProcessor\AsyncFarmManager\` is NOT dead — it's a **standalone Windows Service `FP.AsyncFarmManager`** (own EntryPoint + Settings with per-farm connection string) running in parallel; 2 active jobs (`FarmRebootJob` + `FarmScheduleRebootJob`) with **13× `Thread.Sleep` calls each** (1/5/10s intervals) for machine-control sequencing — registry/network/server-state. Zero cross-refs from other projects confirming operational isolation. Catalogued under `farm-reboots` below.
- `email-notifications` — transactional email sender (welcome / account-deletion / UGC / purchase notifications); SMTP config-driven (localhost:25 default, SSL+auth optional); HTML + inline-image attachments; async fire-and-forget with `RequestContext` preservation for logging.
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\Jobs\Emailing\SendQueuedMailJob.cs` (single job — drains queued outbound mail via `INotificationProvider.GetNotificationsToSend`)
  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Notification\` (~4 files ~80 LOC — `INotificationProvider`: `GetNotificationSettings` / `QueueNotification` / `GetNotificationsToSend` / `MarkNotificationSent`; DTOs `NotificationDto` + `EmailNotificationDto`; `NotificationTypes` enum; shared with `push-notifications`)
  - `Dal\Sql.MsSql\Notification\SqlNotificationProvider.cs` (~73 LOC impl; minimal sproc wrapper)
  - `Shared\Notifications\EmailSender.cs` — static SMTP client + `Initialize(smtpConfig)` + `SendEmail`/`SendEmailAsync` (**not idempotent — second Init overwrites first**).
  - `Shared\Notifications\IEmailSender.cs` (contract — sync return bool + out errorMessage)
  - `Shared\Notifications\EmailNotificationManager.cs` user-facing coordinator — pulls localized subject/body from SQL via `DalFactory.GetNotificationProvider()`; if DB down, silent-fail (logged, no retry).
  - `Shared\Notifications\EmailMessageProducer.cs` template variable-substitution helper.
- `photon-standalone-client` — **Photon client library for inter-server RPC** (misnamed "client" — is server-only). Wraps `PhotonLoadbalancingApi` + `Photon3DotNet` SDK; encapsulates Master/Game/Club server connections, room create/join, pond/location queries, inventory ops, purchases, repairs, game actions, chat. Consumed by `Auth` (Master→Master RPC), `WebAdmin` (Master RPC), `TwitchManager` (Master RPC for drops delivery), game-server tests.
  - `Shared\StandaloneClient\` (16 files): **`PhotonStandaloneClient.cs` (~1300+ LOC main wrapper)** over `StandaloneClientBase` Photon wire-layer; operations CreateGame/JoinGame/JoinRandomGame/LeaveGame/GetProfile/UpdateProfile/BuyItem/License/Repair + game actions (Throw/Cast/Fight/Catch/...) + chat (SendMessage/JoinChatChannel/FindFriends); `PhotonHelper` static factory with retry logic for Master/Pond connections — **hardcoded Master endpoint + 3s hardcoded timeout** + silent-fallback after 5 retries (no DLQ); `PhotonHelperDynamic` instance variant for multi-client scenarios (tournaments, club rooms); `ClubHelper` separate Club factory; 8 request/response DTO helpers (CreateGame/JoinGame/JoinRandomGame × Request/Response + `GameParameter` + `RoomType` enum).
- `farm-reboots` — farm-wide reboot signaling: server subscribes to reboot/cancel events and broadcasts `EventCode.RebootSignal` (remaining time + expected downtime) to all connected clients. Server-admin/infrastructure concern, adjacent to farm management.
  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Async\FarmRebootDto.cs` + `FarmRebootScheduleDto.cs` (reboot-schedule + event records; paired with `Shared\SharedLib\FarmReboots\FarmRebootHelper` DB-poll loop)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncFarmManager\` (**standalone Windows Service `FP.AsyncFarmManager`** — machine-level orchestration side of `farm-reboots`; ~10 files: `EntryPoint.cs` installer + `FarmManagerSettings` with per-farm connection string + `Scheduler\FarmManagerScheduleExecutor.cs` registering 1 active job)
  - `AsyncProcessor\AsyncFarmManager\Jobs\FarmRebootJob.cs` + `FarmScheduleRebootJob.cs` (**heavy `Thread.Sleep`** 13× per job with 1/5/10s intervals for sequencing registry edits + network commands + server-state polling)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\FarmReboots\` (2 files ~200 LOC — **core `farm-reboots` module implementation**): `FarmRebootAdapter.cs` (~71 LOC state-machine — events `OnReboot(TimeSpan remainTime, int expectedDowntime)` + `OnRebootCancel`; state `rebootTime` + `rebootIndex` (0-3) + `rebootStatuses[]` tracks 60/30/10/5-minute thresholds; `ProcessRebootCheck` called by game loop, queries `FarmRebootHelper` current state; detects reboot-time change → resets intervals; on `HasReboot=false` cancel-signal emits `OnRebootCancel` + resets; debouncing via status array); `FarmRebootHelper.cs` (~125 LOC background scheduler — static props `HasReboot`/`RebootTime`/`ExpectedDowntime` shared across adapters; `Start` spawns background thread running `RunUpdateLoop` infinite loop with 100ms sleep; 2-phase — Check Phase 60s queries DAL `GetNextReboot` + `TriggerReboot` if found / Wait Phase 10s polls for cancellation or update, exits when reboot time passes; auto-cancel after 5 min if stale; catches all exceptions; 60-min visibility horizon)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Async\` (2 files ~82 LOC — actually farm-reboots support, misnamed folder): `AsyncHelper.cs` (~21 LOC — static `FarmRebootScheduleDto → FarmRebootSchedule` deserialization helper); `FarmRebootSchedule.cs` (~62 LOC — immutable POCO `(DayOfWeek[] RebootDays, Time[] RebootTimes)` tuple + `ToString`/`ToFineString`/`Equals`/`GetHashCode`)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_FarmReboots.cs` (~43 LOC): `FarmRebootAdapter` lazy property (instantiates `SharedLib.FarmReboots.FarmRebootAdapter`, subscribes `OnReboot` + `OnRebootCancel`); `FarmRebootAdapter_OnReboot(TimeSpan rebootRemainTime, int expectedDowntime)` (~8 LOC — sends `EventCode.RebootSignal` with `rebootRemainTime.Ticks` + `expectedDowntime`); `FarmRebootAdapter_OnRebootCancel` (~6 LOC — sends `EventCode.RebootSignal` with `Flag=false`)
- `dal` **(system)** — data access layer; groups modules: dal-common, dal-abstraction, dal-utilities, dal-log, nosql-file-storage, nosql-interface, nosql-mongo, sql-interface, sql-mssql
  - `Dal\`
- `dal-log` — logging library (including to Mongo) + `Stmt` SQL audit table + 24-channel log factory
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Logging\` (7 files ~1.1k LOC — **user-activity log shipping pipeline** + logger wrappers): `ILoggerWrapper.cs` / `ILogWrapper.cs` (~174 + 265 LOC — `ExitGames.Logging.ILogger` / `log4net.ILog` decorators with `ProcessMessage` pre-processing hook for redaction/filtering); `InventoryLoggingExtensions.cs` (~35 LOC — `LogBuoyOperation` / `LogNavBuoyOperation` / `LogChumRecipeOperation` / `LogRodSetupOperation` append inventory state); **`UserLogsToMongoSync.cs` (~352 LOC primary)** — async filesystem→Mongo log streaming: `Start()` spawns 3 async tasks (periodic `ScheduleSaveSyncStatus` 5s / `ScheduleRescanFiles` 60s + `FileSystemWatcher`) + per-file `MonitorFile` task; file-naming convention `{serverName}.{channelName}-{other}.log` → `LogBase.ToCollectionName(channelName)`; exponential backoff 500ms→60s on empty read; stale-file cleanup (deletes fully-synced logs older than configurable interval, default 2 days); **reflection-hack** accesses `StreamReader` private `charPos`/`charLen`/`charBuffer` to compute true stream position accounting for buffered-unread chars (**.NET-version-fragile**); `Stop()` async with 30s timeout via `Task.WhenAny`. `UserLogsToMongoBuffer.cs` (~70 LOC per-collection `ConcurrentBag` batched flush); `UserLogsToMongoSettings.cs` (~72 LOC — stop timeout / flush intervals / backoff ratios / batch sizes from AppSettings); `UserLogsToMongoStatus.cs` (~107 LOC — file read-position tracker with JSON persistence + .tmp/.bak atomic-rename dance + double-checked locking, uses `System.Text.Json` **inconsistent with Newtonsoft elsewhere**). Consumed by all 4 Photon apps via `AddUserLogsToMongoSynchronization()` extension.
  - `Dal\Dal.Log\Logs\LogCollection.cs` (~212 LOC — factory + log4net configuration; double-checked-lock one-time setup; switches between file-log and Mongo-log backend per `IUserLogParameters.SaveUserLogsToFsEnabled`; file appender uses `MinimalLock` + rolling by size; hardcoded `MaxFileSize = 10GB` + Windows path placeholder `%property{Photon:ApplicationLogPath}\\`)
  - `Dal\Dal.Log\Logs\ILogCollection.cs` (contract — aggregates 24 log channels: Trade / Fishing / Achievement / Tournament / Club / Cheat / Ban / ... — one channel per business domain)
  - `Dal\Dal.Log\Common\StmtLog.cs` (~128 LOC — SQL `Stmt` table writer for currency/move/balance with `requestId` + message; time-range query overload; **`catch (Exception ex)` silently swallows insert failures with log-only**; message auto-truncated to 256 chars without warn)
  - `Dal\Dal.Log\Common\IStmtLog.cs` + `StmtMessage.cs` (contract + DTO)
  - `Dal\Dal.Log\Async\MongoAsyncProvider.cs` (~79 LOC — Mongo TTL cleanup job; **hardcoded store-horizon TimeSpans in static fields**: `MessageStoreHorizon=14d` / `TradesStoreHorizon=90d` / `TelemetryStoreHorizon=7d` / `DebugStoreHorizon=3d` / `IpLogStoreHorizon=180d`; uses **legacy `MongoDB.Driver.Builders.Query` API** — deprecated since C# driver 2.0)
- `dal-common` — data mapping (DB → DTO); `Stats` subfolder measures query duration, read later via PhotonTool; also hosts `RequestContext` thread-static + `AsyncExecutor` fire-and-forget utility + `Crypto` AES wrapper
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\RequestContext.cs` (~25 LOC — `[ThreadStatic]` UserId/RequestId store for cross-layer request tracing; heavily consumed by Dal.Log + Sql.MsSql + NoSql.Mongo; **no thread-safety wrapper** — assumes per-thread model)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\AsyncExecutor.cs` (~50 LOC — `ThreadPool.UnsafeQueueUserWorkItem` fire-and-forget wrapper; **empty `catch {}` ~L15** silently swallows all async-task failures, loses logging)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\Crypto.cs` (~147 LOC — AES/Rijndael password encrypt/decrypt)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\DtoExtensions.cs` (~96 LOC — reflection-based `RestoreObjectFromReader<T>` with type coercion double→float/decimal / int→long/bool / Guid→string; **`PropertyInfo` NOT cached** — `GetProperty` called per row per column, reflection overhead on every read)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\IDalParameters.cs` + `DalParametersProvider.cs` + `AppParametersProvider.cs` + `CustomParametersProvider.cs` + `TestParametersProvider.cs` — connection-string abstraction; reads `app.config` section `"DalParameters"` keys `"sql"` / `"stats"` / `"noSql"`; silent-fail if section/keys missing
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\Stats\OperationStats.cs` (~127 LOC — thread-safe `Interlocked` counters; static `volatile DateTime ResumeTime` / `PauseTime` — **tearing risk on 32-bit** since `DateTime` is 8 bytes and volatile doesn't guarantee atomicity for 64-bit structs)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\Stats\OperationStatsDictionary.cs` (~174 LOC — `ConcurrentDictionary<string, OperationStats>` aggregator)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\Stats\SqlStats.cs` (~202 LOC — `IDbCommand` extension-method tracer; **hardcoded `500ms` + `1000ms` long-query thresholds** for `countLong5` / `countLong10` buckets ~L61-62)
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\Stats\NoSqlStats.cs` — parallel to SqlStats for NoSQL operations
  - `Dal\Dal.Common\Stats\OperationTrace.cs` + `OperationTraceGroup.cs` + `OperationStatsSnapshot.cs` — trace collection DTOs (read via PhotonTool)
- `dal-abstraction` — DI container (service locator/provider) for DAL layer; single static class with ~40 `GetXxxProvider` methods
  - `Dal\DalAbstraction\DalFactory.cs` (~413 LOC — **static service-locator with ~40 `GetXxxProvider()` methods** — Login/Profile/Shop/Tournament/League/Together/etc.); wraps `Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.ServiceProvider`; `InitContainer` hardcoded `MongoDbHelper.Initialize()` coupling; `AddDalServices()` registers all SQL + NoSQL providers as singletons; `AddSqlProvider<T,I>()` generic via `ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance` reflection; **static field `serviceProvider` nullable without guards in getters** (NRE if `InitContainer` not called); **no `Dispose` on ServiceProvider** — resource leak on shutdown; imports 40+ SQL/NoSQL provider namespaces — not a pure abstraction layer
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\DalAdapters\AppInitAdapter.cs` (DAL container init + logging setup)
- `dal-utilities` — ItemFactory: typed DTO factory for inventory system (item types are distinct C# classes)
  - `Dal\DalUtilities\ItemFactory.cs` (~183 LOC — static resolver): `GetTypedItem(InventoryItemDto)` dispatches by `(CategoryId, ConfigJson)` → concrete `Rod` / `Reel` / `FishCage` / `ToolItem` / `OutfitItem` subclass; `ResolveItemType(categoryId)` 2-stage lookup — `ItemSubTypes` enum first, parent-category fallback; `Assembly.GetType(requestedTypeName)` with **string-built typeName** ~L155-161 (fragile, needs exact naming match); **hardcoded manual resolver table** ~L164-181 (Keepnet→FishCage / Tent→ToolItem / ... — must be updated when new item subtypes added); `ItemCategoryCache` lazy-populated via `DalFactory.GetShopProvider()` — **circular dependency** (DalUtilities depended on by game code, which depends on DalFactory); `JsonConvert.DeserializeObject` try/catch **strips original stack trace** with generic "Error parsing InventoryItem.ConfigJson"
- `nosql-file-storage` — log provider: writes to files; a separate service later reads them and ships to MongoDB (paired with `Shared\SharedLib\Logging\UserLogsToMongoSync`)
  - `Dal\NoSql.FileStorage\FileLogBase.cs` (~50 LOC generic base — uses **`System.Text.Json` inconsistent with Newtonsoft elsewhere**; log4net appender per channel; **error-suppression logic with inverted `loggingFailsSkipped < loggingFailsLogged` condition** ~L31-34 — may hide cascading failures; reads `Dal.Common.RequestContext` — cross-layer coupling)
  - `Dal\NoSql.FileStorage\CommonFileLog.cs` (~32 LOC — base impl wrapping User/Message/RequestId; **`LogAsync()` calls `LogInt()` synchronously — misleading API name**)
  - `Dal\NoSql.FileStorage\BanFileLog.cs` / `CheatFileLog.cs` / `ClientDebugFileLog.cs` / `TogetherFileLog.cs` / `TournamentFileLog.cs` — channel-specific subclasses
  - `Dal\NoSql.FileStorage\ClubFileLog.cs` (~46 LOC — has `IsImportant` flag for retention filtering; **`GetAllClubMessages()` throws `NotImplementedException` ~L43** — dead method or incomplete feature; references `ClubMessage` from `NoSql.Interface.Chat` — mixing domain concern into storage layer)
- `nosql-interface` — NoSQL access contracts core (~526 LOC total across 5 subfolders, but **mostly dispersed** to domain modules — only Async/ + Log/ILogBase+IDiagProvider+LogEntries are pure infra here)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Async\INoSqlAsync.cs` (~7 LOC — single `DeleteOldMessages()` background-cleanup contract)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Log\ILogBase.cs` (base log contract: `Log()` + `LogAsync()` — consumed by every domain log)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Log\IDiagProvider.cs` + `LogEntries.cs` (diag composite contract + log-entry container)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Chat\LogMessageBase.cs` (~16 LOC base DTO for all domain logs — UserId / Message / RequestId / Timestamp auto-set to `DT.Helper.UtcNow`; extended by 6 domain-specific DTOs dispersed below)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Chat\LogMessage.cs` (generic log DTO)
  - (all other files disperse — see `messaging` / `chat-server` / `moderation` / `anti-cheat` / `clubs` / `fishing-together` / `competitive` / `debug` / `error-stats` / `auth` / `admin-audit`)
- `nosql-mongo` — MongoDB accessor core (~1.3k LOC total; **mostly dispersed** to domain modules — only Common/ + Log/LogBase are pure infra here); uses **legacy `MongoDB.Driver.Builders.Query` API** throughout (deprecated since driver 2.0+); fire-and-forget `WriteConcern.Unacknowledged` on all diagnostic inserts; millisecond-sampled exception throttling (`ts.Millisecond % 100 == 0` — ~1% of failures logged)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Mongo\Common\MongoAccessorBase.cs` (~26 LOC abstract base — inherits `IDisposable` but **`Dispose()` is empty** ~L22-24; `Database` cached + `Collection` generic getter by `CollectionName`; ctor calls `MongoDbHelper.GetDb()`)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Mongo\Common\MongoDbHelper.cs` (~92 LOC static helper — `Initialize(IDalParameters)` stores config; **`GetDb()` creates new `MongoClient` every call** ~L18-25 — no connection pooling; `ConvertToIsoDates()` recursive helper ~L33-90 — **no callers, dead**)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Mongo\Log\LogBase.cs` (~102 LOC core base — inherits `MongoAccessorBase<LogMessage>` + impl `ILogBase`; **static `IsSyncLogging` ~L18 NOT volatile, NOT locked**; ctor normalizes collection via `ToCollectionName()`; `Log()` / `LogAsync()` inject `RequestContext.RequestId`; `LogInt()` uses `WriteConcern.Unacknowledged` + millisecond-sampled catch; consumed by every domain log)
  - (all other files disperse — see the same target modules as `nosql-interface`)
- `sql-interface` — SQL access contracts core (~290 files ~9.7k LOC total across 31 subfolders, but **mostly dispersed** to domain modules — only Common/ + parts of Sys/ are pure infra here)

- `sql-mssql` — MSSQL provider core (~26k LOC total across 30 subfolders, but **mostly dispersed** to domain modules — only Common/ is pure infra here); CRUD-focused (business logic should live elsewhere); some logic still via inline SQL and stored-procedure calls; dominant pattern: inline SQL + sprocs + ORM-lite extensions; known query-composition risks (see private audit)

- `anti-cheat` — accumulates a "cheat rating" that resets on ban but influences nothing; noisy, ineffective, called from many places; consumes CPU without actually banning anyone. **Evidence confirms ineffective-by-design**: `AntiCheatAdapter.OnUserBanned` event fires when `cheatRatingIncrease > autobanThreshold` but **no handler wired in production** — cheaters pass undetected.
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Chat\CheatMessage.cs` (cheat-event DTO extending `LogMessageBase`)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Interface\Log\ICheatLog.cs` (cheat-log contract)
  - `Dal\NoSql.Mongo\Log\CheatLog.cs` (~60 LOC impl — `FindUserMessages` overloads + `FindMessagesByCheatType` aggregation with **hardcoded `.Take(100)` ~L57**; bypasses `Collection` property via direct `Database.GetCollection<CheatMessage>(CollectionName)` ~L31)
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\AntiCheatAdapter.cs` (~47 LOC per-user cheat-rating accumulator): tracks cumulative `cheatRatingIncrease` via `IncreaseCheatRating` + `HighestCheat` (session worst); events `OnWarning`/`OnCheat(userId, cheatType, message)`/`OnUserBanned`; autoban signal only — **no actual ban execution**.
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\AntiCheatConstants.cs` (~28 LOC cheat severity scale as consts, no enum): `PureCheat=100` / `HighCheat=40` / `MediumCheat=10` / `LowCheat=1` / `NoCheat=0` (for periodic logging).
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\AntiCheatEnums.cs` (~13 LOC `PlayerAction` enum: Throw / Move / FinishAttack / Fight / Catch / TakeOut / ElectricAutoWinding) used by `AntiCheatFishingManager.Update` to route detections by action phase.
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\AntiCheatCommonManager.cs` (~760 LOC **primary common-event detector**): 9 categories — room/pond/tournament/club/FTG mismatch (9.2/9.31-9.39 teleport), permission checks (9.1/9.4.x unauthorized ops/messaging/HTML), inventory cheats (9.5-9.11/9.14-9.20/9.25-9.27 release/repair-on-pond/negative-amounts/time-manipulation), license+tournament (9.17-9.24 min-level/money), **boat cheats** (12.1-12.5/13.0-13.13 rental-days/type-mismatches/boarding/turnover/fast-travel), rowing+stamina (13.3-13.10 dual-action/max-velocity/boat-anomalies). Signal processing: `StrongCheatLoger` (immediate + repeat-delay throttle) vs `WeakCheatLoger` (2 detections within `detectionDelay` sec — reduces false-positives from network jitter). **Hardcoded cheat-codes** ("13.4"/"13.8" etc.) coupled to legacy reporting — renumbering breaks monitoring.
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\AntiCheatFishingManager.cs` (**~993 LOC god-class fishing-specific detector**): 30+ distinct detections across casting (max-distance vs rod+cast-length, "clicker suspected" 1.4-1.5), tackle mechanics (velocity / moves-away / instant-catch 6.1), line/rod (line-longer-than-spool 2.1, extension ratios 2.2-2.3), fishing mechanics (friction > ReelMaxLoad 5.1 impossible-without-hack, reel-while-spool-open 5.3-5.7, electric-reel overload 5.6, landing-net timing 15.1-15.5), **fish-behavior anomalies** (avg-velocity > 5m/s 6.14 too-fast, reel-time-too-short 6.2-6.3, force-ratio < 0.2 over 5 catches 6.5-6.8 "stamina hack", scripted-AI detection 6.7-6.8 fish-goes-to-player > 75%), **bot-detection** (daily > 16h, weekly > 72h active 7.1-7.2), attack distance-anomalies (6.15-6.21 teleport). ~110 private fields for state tracking (`Averager velocityAverager`, 5+ `TimeCounter` trackers, rolling `QueueFloatFilter`/`QueueTimedFilter` for last-N fish/casts). Thresholds empirically tuned (e.g., `MaxTackleAverageVelocity=9f` comment "decided with Dmitriy Ivanov to reduce false-positive"). **`preserveFishTemplate` thread-locked but never unlocked in `Reset`** — stale data forever in long sessions.
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\Averager.cs` (~37 LOC time-weighted moving average: `average = (average*dtTotal + value*dt) / (dtTotal+dt)` EWMA). Correct.
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\HistoryData.cs` (~48 LOC rolling-window session stats): `FishForceData` (last 5 force-ratio+time) + `FishDirectionData` (last 5 movement to/from player) + `LineExtData` (last 3 extension-ratio) + `CastingForceData` (last 20 force values) + `FishAvgVelocityData` (last 5 avg-velocity) + `LineReelOutData` (last 5 reel-ratio) + `TackleYDeltaRatio` (last 5 Y-movement) + `ActiveSeconds` Queue (7-day window). **Double-counts** (FishForceData + FishAvgVelocityData both per-catch).
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\QueueFilter.cs` (~127 LOC generic rolling aggregators): `QueueFilter<T>` with pluggable operators + concrete specializations `QueueFloatFilter`/`QueueDoubleFilter`/`QueueIntFilter` + `QueueTimedFilter` (time-weighted); `Add` (dequeue if full) / `Average` / `CalcStdDeviation` / `IsFull`. **`ReadJson` throws `NotImplementedException`** — dead code. Not thread-safe (no locks).
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\TimeCounter.cs` (~35 LOC ratio-tracker for binary events): `Ratio = timeMatched / (timeMatched + timeNotMatched)`. Correct.
  - `Photon\src-server\AntiCheat\`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\GameProcessor.cs` (66 anti-cheat touchpoints per rod — `antiCheat.PlayerPosition`, `.TacklePosition`, `.ReelSpeed`, `.IsReeling`, `.Update(PlayerAction.*)`, `.RodLength`, `.ReelMaxLoad`, `.MaxLineLength`, `.HistoryData`; `peer.AntiCheatManager.LeavingLocationInImpossibleState()` on exit; uses `AntiCheatFishingManager`)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Helpers\DenuvoProtectionHelper.cs` (extension methods to start/stop Denuvo anti-tamper for Steam/Epic; integrates with `Shared\Denuvo\` project)
  - `Shared\Denuvo\DenuvoHelper.cs` + enums `StartEndPlayStatusCodes`/`SupportedPlatforms` — thin HTTP facade for Denuvo AC-SRV API (`https://ac-srv.codefusion.technology/api/v1/`): `StartPlay`/`EndPlay` match begin/end event reporting for Steam+Epic. **Hardcoded API key in source.**
- `counter-publisher` — Photon app (own .sln) that installs Windows performance counters; Photon is deeply integrated with Windows; Photon docs describe the counters; some are used in monitoring (TODO: document which). **Standalone sidecar** — `CreatePeer` returns null (no client connections), pure publisher of Photon + OS metrics to Windows PerfMon / Zabbix.
  - `Photon\src-server\CounterPublisher\Application.cs` (~109 LOC Photon `ApplicationBase` subclass): `Setup` initializes log4net + creates `CounterPublisher` + registers `SystemCounter` + `SocketServerCounter` classes + `Start`; `TearDown` **empty** (no cleanup).
  - `Photon\src-server\CounterPublisher\SocketServerCounter.cs` (~222 LOC static 50+ Windows PerfCounter readers with `[PublishCounter]` attrs across categories: Common (BytesIn/Out + Connections + Peers + Messages + Buffers) / ENet (reliable/unreliable commands + ACKs + Timeouts + Rate-limiting) / TCP/UDP (Peers + Disconnections by client/app/server/timeout + Datagrams) / Threading (IO/ENet/BusinessLogic thread-counts + queue-depths) / Policy. Each counter = `PerformanceCounterReader(category, name, "_Total")` aggregate.
  - `Photon\src-server\CounterPublisher\SocketServerCounterSchema.cs` (~755 LOC constants-only — nested classes `Common`/`Enet`/`Tcp`/`Threading`/`Udp`/`Policy`/`CLR`/`EndNode`/`Proxy`/`S2S` mapping Photon counter categories/names to Windows PerfMon API strings — ensures typo-free lookup).
  - `Photon\src-server\CounterPublisher\SystemCounter.cs` (~132 LOC OS-level monitoring): `Cpu` per-core + `CpuTotal` aggregate via `CpuUsageCounterReader`; `Memory` AvailableMBytes; network `BytesTotalPerSecond`/`SentPerSecond`/`ReceivedPerSecond` via nested `NetworkInterfaceCounter : ICounter` (enumerates all physical NICs via `PerformanceCounterCategory.GetCategories` + filters Loopback/isatap + sums per-interface). Tight-coupled to Windows PerfMon API (non-portable). **Inefficiency**: `GetInstanceNames` enumerated on every counter read.
  - `Photon\src-server\CounterPublisher\`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Common\ChatWinPerfCouterHelper.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Common\ClubWinPerfCouterHelper.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Common\CommonWinPerfCouterHelper.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\ApplicationStatsPublisher.cs` (game-server side of counter-publisher: builds + sends `UpdateAppStatsEvent` via `ServerEventCode.UpdateAppStats` S2S event to master at `GameServerSettings.Default.AppStatsPublishInterval`; carries `PeerCount` + `GameCount`. Counter-class registration with `CounterPublisher.DefaultInstance.AddStaticCounterClass` in `GameApplication.Setup`.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\ApplicationStats.cs` (master-side aggregator: receives `UpdateAppStats` via `IncomingGameServerPeer.HandleUpdateAppStatsEvent` → `ApplicationStats.UpdateGameServerStats(peer, peerCount, gameCount)`; totals `GameCount` + `PeerCountMaster` + `PeerCountGameServer` + `PeerCount` = sum. Client subscribers (MasterClientPeer) receive `AppStatsEvent` broadcasts over **unreliable UDP** at `AppStatsPublishInterval=5000ms` default.)
- `fish-generator` — spawns fish instances (main orchestrator is 97 KB); reads templates, configures sources (boxes, carousel, scripted, events)

- `bite-system` — fish bite / catch mechanics; core csproj `Shared\BiteSystem\` (~6.4k LOC, 51 prod files); several files in GameModel also belong here. Has a sub-module `bite-system-editor` (pond geometry / boxes editor — was dumped in TravelAdapter but conceptually here). **Anti-cheat-by-design split**: client+server-shared DTOs (Common\) expose only raw weights + pond geometry; server-private logic (ServerOnly\) holds edge distribution + chum boost + form crossover that client cannot predict
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Game\BiteSystemCache.cs` (L2-tier static cache — `InitOnMaster`/`InitOnGame`/`InitOnTech` variants for platform branching; `BiteMaps: CachedEntity<Ponds>` bite-probability engine + `FishFormsCountPerPond` pond→form-count arrays + `PondFishByCode` pond→LocalFish[] by code; subscribes `Caches.OnRefreshDone` for updates)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\Common\ObjectModel\` (~24 files ~2.2k LOC — **client-shared DTOs**): `Pond.cs` (~198 LOC root container — weather dict + fish groups + time charts + probability maps + curves + height/splat/flow maps; `FindMap` / `FindChart` / `FindCurve` / `FindFishGroup` / `GetWaterDepth` / `GetFishWeight` / `GetAllFish`); `BiteMap.cs` (~55 LOC extends `ProbabilityMap` with patch system — first non-zero patch wins, byte→float conversion, modifier scaling); `PondArea.cs` (~37 LOC — geometry **waypoint arrays only**, no polygon/mesh editing; StormArea + SpeedLimitPenalty); `Fish.cs` + `FishData.cs` + `FishDescription.cs` (species + form + weight ranges); `FishGroup.cs` + `FishLayer.cs` (spatial grouping); `HeightMap.cs` + `SplatMap.cs` + `FlowMap.cs` (raster terrain — depth/texture/flow vectors); `BiteMapPatch.cs` + `ProbabilityMap.cs` + `Curve.cs` + `TimeChart.cs` (probability surfaces + interpolation + time modifiers); `Weather.cs` + `WindyMaps.cs` + `TimedMaps.cs` (environmental state); `Settings.cs` + `NormalDistribution.cs` (utility statics + Marsaglia rejection sampling); `AttractorsGroupController.cs` (attractor groups; **`DateTime.Now.Ticks` for RNG seed** — should be `UtcNow`)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\` (~27 files ~4.2k LOC — **server-private logic, anti-cheat-protected**)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\FishWeight\` (~4 files ~450 LOC — fish-weight generation pipeline): `FishWeightGenerator.cs` (~214 LOC — **`Generate()` god-method ~86 LOC L65-151** with 4 piecewise branches no-upper+lower / upper-only / lower-only / both, normalized inverse-CDF split-points for density continuity at zone boundaries) + `FishWeightGeneratorConfig.cs` (~148 LOC immutable snapshot from DB; `static volatile Current` for atomic thread-safe swap; `FromSettings()` clamps zones to [0,1] + 80% overlap-prevention rescale + algo-name → strategy mapping with **silent fallback to `CapAtThreshold` if name doesn't parse** — should warn) + `FishWeightRounding.cs` (~29 LOC — 3-decimal `AwayFromZero` shared across prod + tests) + `FishWeightSimulationService.cs` (Monte Carlo bucket validation tool)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\FishWeight\EdgeDistribution\Strategies\` (~5 files ~130 LOC): `IEdgeDistributionStrategy` interface (`Sample(rnd, u)` + `EdgeAreaFraction` prop); `CapAtThreshold.cs` (~25 LOC — `A=0` mathematically empty, **fail-safe default**); `Unrestricted.cs` (~29 LOC — `A=1` identity, no redistribution); `PowerLawEdge.cs` (~53 LOC — `p(s)=(1-s)^α`, `A=1/(α+1)`, hard boundary at max weight, `α` clamped 1e-10); `ExponentialEdge.cs` (~55 LOC — `p(s)=e^(-λs)`, `A=(1-e^-λ)/λ`, asymptotic falloff theoretically unbounded, `λ` clamped 1e-10, **no `u=1.0` guard** in test path)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\FishSelector.cs` (large ~700 LOC) — **8 public mutable static fields** (`StepsToGenerateFloatFish=6` / `ProbabilityForFloatAttractionPoint=0.015` / etc.) **NOT volatile** — race risk if `GlobalVariables` reloads mid-generation; computes bite probability via `ProbabilityDetails` struct (maps + attractors + chum + time charts)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\ActiveAttractor.cs` (runtime attractor state — position + efficiencies + decay)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\ChumSystem.cs` (~100+ LOC static factory — `AddChumObject` / `UpdateChum` / `RemoveChumObject`; subscribes to object updates)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\ChumObject.cs` + `ChumPiece.cs` (feeder state + particles + decay over time + position tracking)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\CaughtFishDetractor.cs` (caught-fish bite-probability penalty — `detractionType` Add/Mul + `detractionDuration`)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\PlayerData.cs` (~100 LOC — per-player state: RNG seed via `new Random(Guid.NewGuid().GetHashCode())` — **non-reproducible across .NET versions, debugging-hostile** + `AllGeneratedFish[]` + 7-rod `FishSelector[]` + `Attractors` + `ChumObjects` + `FishDetractors`)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\IBiteMap.cs` (server-side bite-probability query interface) + `MockBiteMap.cs` (test stub)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\PondServer.cs` (~partial Pond — `HandleCatchFish` / `OnThrown` / `GetActiveFishZones` / ChumSystem integration; **hardcoded `_distWeight2Probabilities` array L16-22** distances [1,5,10,30] → scalars [1, 0.6, 0.3, 0.01] — unexplained magic; commented-out `GlobalVariablesCache` + `FishCache` references L109-110 — dropped)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\FishRadarSettings.cs` (radar config tied to bite-system data)
  - `Shared\BiteSystem\ServerOnly\Helpers\DataConverter.cs` line ~50 — **`WriteJson` throws `NotImplementedException`** — read-only converter, dead write path
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\AutoHookModel.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\Hooker.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\LiveBaitModel.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\RodInGameConfig.cs` (computes per-rod bite chance — primary here; also touches game-model-core)
- `bite-system-editor` — pond geometry + fish/hitch/stream box editor with audit trail; client-side 3D geometry syncs to DB. Part of `bite-system`. Lives in TravelAdapter historically for no good reason.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\DalAdapters\TravelAdapter.cs` (methods: `UpdatePondGeometry`, `UpdateHitchBoxes`, `GetPondGeometry`, `DecodeGeometry`, `GetFishCodeNames`)
- `hitches` — tackle-hitch mechanic: rig gets caught on HitchBoxes (designated snag zones) or on the bottom (based on SplatMap layer). `Unhitch` resolves by force (CanBreak + force > MaxLoad) or probability. Also generates **underwater items** (sunken items the player can recover by snagging). Modes: dead hitch (can't unhitch), bottom hitch, box hitch. Part of `bite-system` (configured in the same editor; engages the rod similarly).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\HitchGenerator.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\GameProcessor.cs` (hitch integration in `HandleMove` — box detection, bottom-hitch generation, IsHitch state flag)
- `fish-fight` — player-vs-fish struggle once hooked (hooking = moment fish-fight starts); fish stamina/tire model; strong-fish escape chance (time-rolling probability after guaranteed fight period); fight-inactivity detection; escape-on-room-end teleportation
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\Fish\` (FishTireModel)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\StrongFishEscapeModel.cs` (static feature toggle + per-fight state; kicks in when playerForce/fishForce < limitForce)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\GameProcessor.cs` (fish-fight driver methods: `HandleFightFish` (173 LOC), `HandleAttackFinished` (189 LOC — strike validation = hooking; also does license check which leaks from `licenses`), `FightFishInactivityCheck`, `EscapeFishOnRoomEnd` (262 LOC), `UpdateFishTire`, `InitFishTire`, `InitElectricOverload`, `InitHugeFishDisplay`)
- `wear` — gear deterioration across three layers: (1) runtime per-action wear during fishing (Rod/Reel/Line/Leader/Hook/Bobber with tier-multipliers 1x/2x/3x/4x at 50/75/100% load, critical wear per-tick above 100%, tooth-sharpness multiplier, bottom-contact wear for leader); (2) break/cut mechanics during fight under tension, slack, teeth sharpness; (3) daily wear on equipped/used inventory items at end of day (saltwater penalty). Part of `inventory` system.
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\LeaderBreaker.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\LeaderCutterOnLineSlack.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\LeaderCutterOnLineTension.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\LineBreaker.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\DalAdapters\InventoryAdapter.cs` (method `GenerateDailyWear` — daily wear loop with saltwater multiplier)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\WearSystem.cs` (runtime per-FishingAction wear engine; enums `TackleType`, `FishingAction`; emits `OnWear` event)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\GameProcessor.cs` (7 nearly-identical `ApplyWearTo{Rod,Reel,Line,Leader,Hook,...}` methods + `UpdateWearSystem` + breakage — `BreakLineLoseTackle` (108 LOC), `BreakLeaderLoseTackle` (66 LOC); subscribes `WearSystem.OnWear` events from inside GameProcessor)
- `game-model-core` — shared game-simulation primitives, converters, helpers, stats telemetry
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Common\` (23 files ~1.5k LOC: Amount + Point3/Point2/Box geometry + BaitColorPattern + CachedValue + CollectionUtilities + SerializationHelper — base primitives)
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Helpers\` (14 files ~1.8k LOC: `ChangeTracker` ITrackable visitor pattern + DateTimeExtensions + EnumHelper + utility mixins)
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Randomization\` (5 files ~292 LOC: CryptoRandom + DeterministicRandom + IRandom + RandomType)
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Serialization\` (23 files ~1.6k LOC: ClientObjectModelBinder + CompressHelper + DerivedOnlyContractResolver + AmountFromStringConverter; **`OneLinePointConverter.ReadJson` throws `NotImplementedException`** L150 write-only)
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\CurrentGameConfig.cs` (~375 LOC per-game session config aggregator — central snapshot for fishing session). Collections: `FishCache Dict<FishId, ServerFish>` pond-lookup, `FishBoxes`/`MissionFishBoxes` + `HitchBoxes`/`MissionHitchBoxes` spatial condition boxes (time+weather), `LocationFish` fallback, `Accelerators` time/weather attack-rate boosters, `BiteSystemData` PlayerData. Computed props: `ActiveFishBoxes` within `MaxCastLength+15m`, `TimeOfDay` via `InGameTimeHelper`, `GetActiveAccelerators` LINQ time-of-day+weather filter. `LookupFish` dynamic-fish filter via `activeDynamicFish` set. `ResetActiveFishBoxes` invalidates on player-move > 5m.
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\RodInGameConfig.cs` (~200 LOC per-rod session state). Debug flags (DebugNoFish / DebugAlwaysHook / DebugFishId / DebugBiteTime); tackle composition (Rod + Reel + Line + Leader + Hook + JigHead + Sinker + Baits); computed `LineOrLeaderVisibility` (schedule or const) / `LineOrLeaderMaxLoad` (min of line+leader) / `IsBarbless` / `IsCurrentDragIgnored`. **Shared with `bite-system`** (per-rod bite-chance computation).
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\Converters\Converters.cs` (~91 LOC JSON converters for game-model primitives — `OneLineAcceleratorConverter` serializes `BaitAccelerator`/`BaitColorAttraction`/`DragAttraction` to compact single-line + `OneLineArrayOfstringsConverter`; **deserialization throws `NotImplementedException`** — write-only converters).
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\Helpers\GameUtils.cs` (~101 LOC stateless utilities): `CheckCondition(condition, pondTime, weather, isMissionFishBox)` time-of-day+weather match with night-wrap; `RandomizeFishWeight(min, max, bias, rnd)` weight-bias distribution (Min→half-normal / Max→1-half-normal / linear); `GetCooldown`/`WarmupBox`/`CooldownBox` cooldown-item filtering by pond+box ID with warmup-rate.
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\Helpers\NormalRandom.cs` (~181 LOC seeded-RNG with normal-distribution): `NextLinearFloat/Decimal` linear; `NextLinearFloat(operation)` with dedup (rejects if diff < 0.1); `NextLinearInt4Attack(min, max)` history-dedup (avoids repeat last 2 attacks); `NextNormal`/`NextHalfNormal`/`NextFullNormal` Box-Muller; `RandomElement<T>`; seeded via `Guid.NewGuid().GetHashCode` (non-deterministic, `RngSeed` exportable).
  - `Photon\src-server\GameModel\Stats\FishStatsAdapter.cs` (~155 LOC async telemetry — fish lifecycle recorder via `saveActionScheduler` async-wrapper). 6 ops: `SaveFishGenerated(Source, weight, pond, playerLevel, rodConfig, distance, weather, location)` (**18 parameters — long list**), `SaveFishGone(reason, baitConsumed)`, `SaveFishHooked(distance, strikingFlags)`, `SaveFishEscaped(distance, reason, fightDuration)`, `SaveFishCaught(fightDuration, xp, silver)`, `SaveEquipmentBroken(fightDuration)`. Kill switch `EnvironmentVariableCache.CollectFishGenerationStats`.
- `master-server` **(app)** — main load-balancer-facing entry point for clients; auth gateway; client-to-game-server redirect router; room-registry liaison (receives `UpdateGame/RemoveGame` events from all connected game-servers and maintains the `game-rooms` Lobby registry via `Lobby\` + `ChannelLobby\` subfolders); app-stats aggregator. Inbound S2S from game-servers via `IncomingGameServerPeer`. Outbound S2S to chat-server via `ChatEnabledApplication` base. Two-node cluster pattern: one master node (`IsMaster=true`) handles all client ops; slave node runs `RedirectedClientPeer` that immediately redirects clients to the master. Note: this MasterServer folder contains a small `GameApplication.cs` — it's NOT the game-server's GameApplication, just a misleadingly-named helper class for the lobby-owning application context ("Default" app).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\MasterApplication.cs` (~439 LOC — `class MasterApplication : ChatEnabledApplication`, app bootstrap). Owns `AppStats` (static `ApplicationStats`), `GameServers` (`GameServerCollection`), `LoadBalancer<IncomingGameServerPeer>` (loads `LoadBalancer.config`), `DefaultApplication` (GameApplication "Default" — the lobby-owning context), `Peers` (PeerList), `LocalNodeId`/`MasterNodeId`/`IsMaster` (master-node election via `Nodes.txt`). Constructor: reads chat-server address from `MasterServerSettings`, S2S custom-type cache. `Setup()` — `InitLogging` + `Initialize()` + `DebugUsersCache.Start`. `Initialize()` — `PlatformMapping.Initialize`, `AppInitAdapter.InitializeDal/Initialize`, clears disconnect signals; **~18 caches in 3 tiers** (tier 0 ~13 independent incl. `AbTestCache`/`EnvironmentVariableCache`/`GlobalVariablesCache`/`JsonVariablesCache`/`EulaCache`/`FishCache`/`GameServerCache`/`InitialProfileCache`/`ItemCategoryCache`/`LicenseCache`/`StatesCache`/`SkinsCache`/`UsernamePartsCache`; tier 1 `EventCache`/`ItemCache`/`ItemAssetCache`/`MonetizationCache`/`RewardsCache`; tier 2 `AchievementsCache`/`BiteSystemCache`/`LevelingCache`); `InGameTimeHelper.Init` + `CacheRefreshHelper.Start`; `EmailSender.Initialize`; creates `GameServerCollection` + `LoadBalancer` + `DefaultApplication`; conditional `ApplicationStats` if `AppStatsPublishInterval>0`; `InitResolver()` (`Nodes.txt` → `LocalNodeId` + `MasterNodeId` — 0→0, else→1); 6 platform cert helpers (Apple/Android/Epic/Xbox/Steam/Nintendo); `DisconnectSignalProcessor.Start`; `StatisticEventsHive.Init+Start`; `DalFactory.GetFishingTogetherProvider().RefreshSuspendedSessions`; `AddUserLogsToMongoSynchronization`. `CreatePeer(InitRequest)` factory dispatches: port 4520 → `IncomingGameServerPeer`; IsMaster → `MasterClientPeer`; slave → `RedirectedClientPeer`. `OnStopRequested` — stops `DebugUsersCache` + disconnects all GameServers peers. `TearDown` — stops CacheRefreshHelper / DisconnectSignalProcessor / StatisticEventsHive + awaits userLogsSync.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\MasterClientPeer.cs` (**~1689 LOC god-class — per-client peer on master**, `class MasterClientPeer : Peer` implements `ILobbyPeer`/`IGenericPeer`/`IClubPeer`). room ops (`HandleCreateGame` ~30 LOC enqueues to lobby, **`HandleJoinGame` ~50 LOC** with **friend-room special logic** — if `GameId==TopFriendsRoomName`: load profile friends, `TravelAdapter.GetRoomsPopulation`, filter by language, sort by friend count);   - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\GameServer\IncomingGameServerPeer.cs` (~728 LOC — **mirror of `OutgoingMasterServerPeer` in game-server**, `class : InboundS2SPeer`). Identity: `ServerId` / `Key` (IP:UDP:TCP); address props (TCP/UDP/WS/HTTP + IPv6 + secure variants); load state `LoadLevel` (FeedbackLevel) + `State` (ServerState: Normal/OutOfRotation/Offline) + `PeerCount`; `LastActivity`/`LastOperation`; lazy `PerformanceAdapter`. **`HandleRegisterGameServerRequest` (~140 LOC god)** — validates contract, guards `!IsMaster` → returns RedirectRepeat, extracts+stores all addresses/hostnames/ports, formats with proper prefixes (`ws://`/`https://`/etc.), validates hostname for HTTPS/WSS, sets ServerId + State, calls `GameServerCollection.OnConnect`, **adds to `LoadBalancer` if State==Normal**, starts `MonitorLoop` (1s interval heartbeat watchdog), response carries AuthList + SharedKey + InternalAddress. **3 inbound event handlers**: `UpdateServer` (~58 LOC — updates LoadLevel/PeerCount, Normal↔OutOfRotation↔Offline state-transitions, refreshes LoadBalancer, resets heartbeat-delay flag on recovery); `UpdateGameState` (→ `application.DefaultApplication.OnGameUpdateOnGameServer` → lobby add/update room); `RemoveGameState` (→ `application.DefaultApplication.OnGameRemovedOnGameServer` → lobby remove); `UpdateAppStats` (→ `MasterApplication.AppStats.UpdateGameServerStats`). **Heartbeat watchdog MonitorLoop** (~L546-631): if no `UpdateServer` event for >`GameServerHeartbeatTimeoutSeconds` (global variable), sets `delayUpdateServerStateDetected=true` + changes state to OutOfRotation + **writes TCP address to `Flags\UpdateServerStateDelay` file** (read by game-servers via their file-based state machine — coordination without DB; 200ms × 5 retry on file contention); deletes file on recovery. Disconnect: `RemoveGameServerPeerOnMaster` (removes from GameServerCollection + LoadBalancer + `application.RemoveGameServerFromLobby` for lobby cleanup) + stops monitor loop + flushes perf stats. Commented-out `////RemoveGameServerPeerOnMaster();` on Offline state — soft-offline retention (intentional?).

- `game-server` **(app)** — main worker node; hosts all game logic; players spend most of their connection time here. **Owns the `GameClientPeer` mega-class** — a `partial` class spanning **27 sibling files / ~1.14 MB** of code. Per-player peer backbone: one `GameClientPeer` instance per connected player. Inherits `LitePeer`, implements `IGenericPeer`, `IProfilePeer`, `IFishRadarHost`. The main partial (142 KB, 2882 LOC) owns the client → server operation routing dispatcher (`OnOperationRequest` → `ProcessOperationRequest` → realtime / sync / async pipelines, 50+ operation codes). Also owns shared state (session IDs, profile, adapters, fibers, transaction lock). Multiple modules have **inline** code here instead of their own partial — see leak paths below and section N.

**`OnStopRequested` (~116 LOC graceful shutdown)** — single wrapping try/catch; dispose retry timers; stop WorkloadController + S2S disconnects + base shutdown; offline phase (60s `MaxOfflineTimeout` — broadcasts `RaiseOfflineEvent` via room-enumeration loop with 1s `Thread.Sleep` progress, `ShutdownProgressNotificationTimeout=10s` log cadence); `SuspendFishingTogetherSessions` + `ForceSuspendFishingTogetherSessions`; shutdown phase (30s `MaxShutdownTimeout` — `RaiseShutdownEvent`); `TearDown()` (~24 LOC) — stop processors, disconnect S2S peers, `userLogsSync.Stop().GetAwaiter().GetResult()` (**sync-over-async**), base teardown. **Peer factory**: `CreatePeer(InitRequest)` → single route to `GameClientPeer` via `CreateGamePeer`; `CreateServerPeer(type)` dispatch for Master/Club/Chat; `OnServerConnectionFailed` routes S2S failures to Master/Club reconnect or `WorkloadController.OnLatencyMonitorConnectFailed`. **`CheckGames` (~11 LOC)** — periodic 60s room health check (enumerate `GameCache.Instance` rooms, enqueue check-game message). `DoForAllPeers(string, Action<GameClientPeer>, Func<bool>, bool)` — broadcast utility (SafeEnqueue across `Peers`). `DumpCounterStats` — `StatisticEventsHive` callback routing `connect`/`disconnect`/`send` counts to `DalFactory.GetAnalyticsProvider().DumpConnectStats`/`DumpEmailSendStats`. Global state: `Peers`, `GlobalLeaguesContext`, static `masterPeer`/`clubPeer` (thread-safe via `Interlocked.Exchange`), `AppStatsPublisher`, `WorkloadController`, `S2SCacheMan`.
- `chat-server` **(app)** — message bus; originated as chat server, now also carries inter-server / service messages. Transport-agnostic router: it detects message *envelope* (1-to-1 vs group vs channel) and routes accordingly — it does NOT interpret the ~40 message-type codes (that dispatch lives on the game-server side in `GameClientPeer_Messaging.ProcessMessageSafeActions`). Three logical subsystems inside one module: **message pipeline** (`ChatProcessor` + 3 queues), **channel engine** (`ChannelMemoryCache` + `ChatChannel`), **presence engine** (`PlayerCache2` + `GameServerCollection`).
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Chat\` (4 files ~195 LOC — `ChatLogic` static persistence helpers + ChatMessageBase + PrivateChatMessage DTO)
  - `Shared\Photon.Interfaces\Chat\ChatSubOperationCode.cs` (~16 LOC — SendChatCommand/SendChatMessage/ConfirmChatMessage/GetChatPlayersCount/GetChatMessages)

  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Chat\IPrivateChatMessagesProvider.cs` + `IOfflineMessagePersister.cs` + `PrivateChatMessageDto.cs` + `OfflineMessageDto.cs` (SQL side of chat: private-message history + offline-queue persistence)

  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ChatServer\ChatApplication.cs` (~259 LOC — `class ChatApplication : ApplicationBase`, app bootstrap). Owns singletons `ChatProcessor` (lock-guarded getter/setter), `GameServers` (`GameServerCollection`), `OnlinePlayers` (`PlayerCache2`), `ChannelMemoryCache`, `S2SCustomTypeCacheMan`, `userLogsSync`. `Setup()` → `Initialize()` — creates collections + pond-channels via `DalFactory.GetTravelProvider()` pond IDs, subscribes cache refresh; `StartMessageRelay()` builds `ChatProcessor` with fluent config: `UseDefaultConfiguration()` (TTLs + retry counts) + `UseThreadPoolExecutor()` + `UseDatabaseRecipientResolver()` (lazy username→GUID via `DalFactory.GetLoginProvider().GetUserIdByName`) + `UsePhotonSender()` (routes via `IncomingGameServerPeer.SendEvent`) + `UseAnalyticsExceptionHandler()` + `UseGiftPushNotification()`; starts pipeline. Public API: `EnqueueChatMessage` / `ConfirmChatMessage`. `OnStopRequested` — `StopMessageRelay` with 10s wait, disconnects all game-server peers. `TearDown` — stops `CacheRefreshHelper` + `userLogsSync`.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ChatServer\Processing\ChatProcessor.cs` (**~929 LOC god-class** — message pipeline). Three-stage pipeline fields `incomingQueue` + `delayedQueue` + `offlineQueue` + `confirmations: ConcurrentDictionary<messageId, bool>` + maintenance `thread` (1s cycle) + `resetEvent` + `ScanInterval=30s`. Constructor deps: `IOfflineMessagePersister db` (NoSQL/Mongo via `DalFactory.GetOfflineMessagePersister()`), `PlayerCache2 playersCache`, `ChannelMemoryCache channels`. `IMessageProcessor` impl: `Enqueue(ChatMessage)` (if `IsOffline` → `Executor(InsertMessageOffline)` + `incomingQueue.Enqueue`; else direct), `Reenqueue` (resets `RetryCount=0`), `ProcessMessage` (wrapped in Executor), `Confirm(id)` (sets `confirmations[id]=true` + `Executor(Db.RemoveMessage)`), `ProcessPushNotifications`, `OnException`. **State machine** `ProcessMessageSync → ProcessChatMessageSafe → ProcessChatMessage` (core routing ~144 LOC) returns `MessageProcessingStatus` — 6 states: `Suppressed` / `Processed` / `Delivered` / `Confirmed` / `Delayed` / `Offline`. Routing logic: 1) TTL checks (online=`MessageTtl` 300s / channel=`ChannelMessageTtl` 7d / offline `Expiration`) + `ProcessAt > now` → Delayed; 2) group messages (`Group != null`) — detect via `ChatGlobals.IsClubGroup/UndisqualifiedClub/FishingTogether/Custom` + `ChatAdapter.Get{AllActivePlayers/ClubMembers/UndisqualifiedClubMembers/FishingTogetherMembers/GroupMembers}` + `SplitMessage` (clone per recipient, enqueue with `MessageProcessingSource.Group{AllPlayers/AllOnlinePlayers/Club/UClub/FT/Id}`) → Processed; 3) channel messages — `ChannelMemoryCache.GetOrCreateChannel` + `channel.ProcessMessage` → enqueue-to-each-participant → Processed; 4) confirmations dict check → Confirmed; 5) recipient resolve (GUID vs username-lookup); 6) online check via `playersCache.LookupPlayer`: offline → retry-delayed-or-offline-or-suppressed (IsOneTime branch + RetryCount vs `MessageMaxRetryCount=5`), online → `Sender(message, playerState)` via `SendMessage` → `ChatMessageEvent` → `playerState.Game.GameServer.SendEvent`. Retry config: `NextDeliveryRetryIfNoPlayer=15s` + `NextDeliveryRetryIfNoConfirmation=60s` + `NextDeliveryRetryIfException=10s`. Lifecycle: `Start()` — thread + 3 queues + `PlayersCache.OnJoinedEvent` subscribe + async `RestoreQueue()` (load persisted offline from Mongo + deserialize + re-enqueue to OfflineQueue); `Stop` reverses. Push: `GeneratePushNotification` delegate; `UseGiftPushNotification()` handles `ChatRequests.Gift` via `PushNotificationsAdapter` (new instance per message — perf concern). `PushCountPerUserCache` for push-throttling (30s cleanup). `GetStats` returns pipeline stats (enqueue/processing times + durations).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ChatServer\Processing\IncomingQueue.cs` (~159 LOC — FIFO `ConcurrentQueue<ChatMessage>` for fresh inbound; dedicated thread dequeues → `Processor.ProcessMessage`; 1s polling + `resetEvent` signal; `WaitForEmptyQueue` for graceful shutdown; `ChatWinPerfCouterHelper.SetChatMessagesCount` perf counter)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ChatServer\Processing\DelayedQueue.cs` (~184 LOC — time-ordered retry via `ConcurrentSortedQueue<ChatMessage>` with `ProcessAtChatMessageComparer` (ascending `ProcessAt`); dedicated thread dequeues messages where `ProcessAt <= now` + intelligent sleep computing delay to next-ready or 1s default; mark with `MessageProcessingSource.DelayedTime`)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ChatServer\Processing\OfflineQueue.cs` (~294 LOC — per-recipient `ConcurrentDictionary<userId, PriorityChatMessageQueue>` (inner class extending `ConcurrentSortedQueue<ChatMessage>` with `-x.IsPriority.CompareTo(y.IsPriority)` comparator — priority messages first). Dedicated thread monitors (1) player-join events (via `OnPlayersJoined` from PlayerCache2), (2) periodic 30s scan (from ChatProcessor), (3) push notification generation. `Enqueue` atomic `AddOrUpdate` per-user bucket; `OnScanRequired`; `OnPlayersJoined(userIds[])`; `ScanForOnlinePlayers` (resend offline via `Processor.Reenqueue` with `OfflineScanOnline`); `ScanForExpiredMessages` (iterate + remove where `now > Expiration`, `OfflineExpired`); `ScanForPushNotifications`. Tracks `OfflineCount` + `PriorityCount` perf counters)
