- `load-balancer` — collects load/health info from game-servers (they report state); routes new players to the least-loaded game-server. Also includes Photon-SDK load-shedding: `WorkloadController` reads server counters (CPU, RAM, bytes I/O, queue depth, TCP/UDP peers, disconnect rates) and feeds a feedback-control system that outputs `FeedbackLevel` for throttling / request shedding under load.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\LoadBalancer\`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Common\NodesReader.cs` (node ID → IP mapping, watched file)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameApplication.cs` (game-server side of load-balancer integration: `SetupFeedbackControlSystem` (~16 LOC) — creates `WorkloadController(this, PhotonInstanceName, "LatencyMonitor", latencyEndpointTcp, latencyEndpointUdp, 1, 1000, GameServerSettings.Default.MaxCcu)`; dev-server flag disables enforcement via `IsWorkloadControlOff=true`; `OptimizeStartup` skips Init/Start. Latency endpoint resolution: `GetLatencyEndpointTcp` (~54 LOC) / `GetLatencyEndpointUdp` (~54 LOC) — resolve from `LatencyMonitorAddress`/`Udp` or fall back to `PublicIpAddress` + `RelayPortTcp`/`Udp` (or `GamingTcpPort` offset by node ID); validates IP/port. `OnServerConnectionFailed` routes unknown S2S endpoint failures to `WorkloadController.OnLatencyMonitorConnectFailed`.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\LoadShedding\` (Photon-SDK feedback-control load-shedding: `WorkloadController`, `FeedbackControlSystem`/`FeedbackController`/`FeedbackControllerCollection`, enums `FeedbackName`/`FeedbackLevel`/`FeedbackLevelOrder`, `IFeedbackControlSystem`, `ValueHistory`, `AverageCounterReader`, `Configuration\*` (7 files, config-section-based), `Diagnostics\Counter.cs`) — actual usage unverified; see section L
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\MasterApplication.cs` (master-side load-balancer consumer: owns `LoadBalancer<IncomingGameServerPeer>` instantiated from `LoadBalancer.config`; populated when game-servers register via `IncomingGameServerPeer.HandleRegisterGameServerRequest` (if `State==Normal` → `LoadBalancer.TryAddServer`); refreshed on every `UpdateServer` inbound event from game-servers)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\GameServer\GameServerState.cs` (immutable `(LoadLevel, PeerCount)` with `IComparable` operators `>`/`<` — sort key for **least-loaded** game-server selection during new-room placement; `game-rooms` ↔ `load-balancer` cross-module touch point; see `game-rooms` module for the placement policy side)
- `server-to-server` — outbound S2S peers from `game-server` app to `master-server` / `club-server` / `chat-server`, with reconnect + status-query + disconnect lifecycle. Chat leg is inherited via `ChatEnabledApplication` base class. Master & Club legs are directly owned here. Three concrete peers — one per target service — all inherit `OutboundS2SPeer` (Photon SDK) and share the registration-handshake + IsRegistered + reconnect pattern, but serve very different consumer modules.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Common\ChatEnabledApplication.cs` (base: owns `ChatPeer` via `CreateChatPeer()` override; Chat endpoint + connect/disconnect)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Common\OutgoingChatServerPeerBase.cs` (S2S peer base to chat-server)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ServerToServer\` (S2S protocol plumbing — Events + Operations; see folder-tree note for module-wise dispatch)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameApplication.cs` (S2S connection lifecycle): **static** `masterPeer` / `clubPeer` (thread-safe via `Interlocked.Exchange` in property setters); volatile flags `isReconnectingToMaster` / `isReconnectingToClub` (byte — 0=first-time, 1=reconnecting); per-peer retry infrastructure (`masterConnectRetryTimerLock` / `masterConnectRetryTimer` + Club mirror); factories `CreateMasterPeer` / `CreateClubPeer` + `CreateChatPeer` (ChatEnabledApplication override); `CreateServerPeer(type)` dispatch (Master/Club/Chat) clearing reconnect flags; `ConnectToMaster(IPEndPoint)` / parameterless / `ReconnectToMaster` (single-shot `Timer` guarded by lock) / `UpdateMasterEndPoint` (DNS resolve `GameServerSettings.MasterIPAddress`, IPv4-only); mirrored `ConnectToClub` / `ReconnectToClub` / `UpdateClubEndPoint`; status queries `MasterConnectionStatus` / `ClubConnectionStatus` (return `"NULL"` when peer null); `DisconnectMaster` / `DisconnectClub` (check `ConnectionState.Connected` before `Disconnect()`); `OnServerConnectionFailed(errorCode, errorMessage, state)` (~42 LOC — routes failure to Master/Club reconnect vs WorkloadController delegation, first-fail=Error / reconnect=Warn); **dev-only `ImitateClubServiceStopThread`** (static Thread — simulates club service disconnect when `LeaguesAdapter.ImitateClubServiceStop` true on dev-server; logs "Club service disconnect IMITATION" every 2s)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\OutgoingMasterServerPeer.cs` (~420 LOC, **unidirectional (with redirect)**): S2S to `master-server`. Outbound: `RegisterGameServer` (Register() L330 — public IP + TCP/UDP/WS/HTTP ports offset by node ID + serverId + serverState + IPv6), `UpdateServer` event (~1s heartbeat via `updateLoop = RequestFiber.ScheduleOnInterval(1000)`) with `LoadIndex=FeedbackLevel` + PeerCount + ServerState, `UpdateGameState` + `RemoveGameState` events (per-room). Inbound response: `HandleRegisterGameServerResponse` — Ok → `IsRegistered=true` + `UpdateAllGameStates()` + start 1s loop; `RedirectRepeat` → `Reconnect(address)` to new master node (leader election). `UpdateAllGameStates` enqueues `ReinitializeGameStateOnMaster` message to every room in `GameCache.Instance`. **File-based state machine** (~L112-185): reads `Flags\OutOfRotation` + `Flags\StopUpdateServerState`, writes `Flags\PeerCount` + `Flags\LoadLevel` for external monitoring; gated by `fileLock` (Monitor-based) + `isOutOfRoration` instance flag (typo in field name). `EncodeFeedbackLevel` returns human-readable strings ("Full"/"Empty"/"High"/"Low"/"Normal" — misleading name). `OnEvent` + `OnOperationRequest` stubs (master never initiates either). On disconnect → `application.ReconnectToMaster()` unless `redirected` flag set.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\OutgoingChatServerPeer.cs` (~708 LOC, **bidirectional message bus**, extends `OutgoingChatServerPeerBase`): S2S to `chat-server`. Base provides offline outbound queue, `SendMessage(ChatMessageRequest)`, `ConfirmMessageDelivery(messageId)`. Outbound: `RegisterGameServer` handshake; after Ok → `SendAllPlayers()` syncs all current room players to chat-server. Inbound `SendChatMessage` event → `HandleIncomingMessage` → lookup Room + Actor → `peer.EnqueueSafeAction` → **`ProcessMessageSafeActions` (~430 LOC god-method)** — giant if-else chain over `messageEvent.Data` string code (~40+ message types) dispatching to per-module peer handlers. Full routing table (grouped by consumer module): `clubs` (13 handlers — `ChatServer_HandleClubMembersCountChanged` / `LogoChanged` / `CardChanges` / `Invitation` / `Event` / `JoinRequestCreated/Removed/Approved/Declined` / `Kicked` / `Disbanded` / `PlayerClubBanned/Unbanned` + `ClubAdapter.___ReceiveClubChannelExpiration`); `leagues` (5 — `ProcessLeagueChampResult` / `ProcessLeagueSeasonResult` / `ProcessPlayerLeaguesBanned` / `Unbanned` / `EarnClubPoints(source=Debug)`); `UGC` (11 — `UGCHost/Public/Player.Receive_Competition*` + `NotifyClientAboutUserCompetition*` pairs for Promotion/Approved/Declined/Removed/Cancelled/Started/Reverted/Invitation/InvitationResponse/Exchange/ExchangeResponse); `messaging` (`OnReceiveMessage_Friendship`); `fishing-together` (`OnOutboundEvent_Together`); `leaderboards` (`OnReceiveMessage_Leaderboards`); `tournaments` (`ProcessTournamentResult` / `ProcessTournamentCancellation`); `product-delivery` (`DeliverPendingItems` / `ProcessProductDelivery`); `missions` (`ProcessMission` + post-handler `ProcessMissions`); `gifting` / `buoys` / `presets` / `chum` (`ProcessGift` / `ProcessBuoy` / `ProcessPreset` / `ProcessChumRecipe` — each with inline Xbox-gold-required guard `PlatformMapping.DefaultPlatformId == SharedConsts.XBoxPlatformId && !peer.HasMultiplayerPriv`); `moderation` (`HandleChatBan`); `rewards` (`ProcessGiveReward`); `profile-management` (`SaveProfileWithLog("ForceSave")` / `ProcessProfileFlag`); `debug` (`HandleDebugConfig`); `competitions-lifecycle` (`ProcessCompetitionsBan`); UGC flags (`UGC_ProcessIsUgcHost` / `UGC_ProcessIsInfluencer`); tournaments (`SendEvent(TournamentLogoRequested)`). Each handler sets `ctx.Send` (echo-to-client) + `ctx.ImmediateConfirm` (ACK-now); post-dispatch `peer.ProcessTargetedAds()` + optionally `peer.ProcessMissions()`. Duplicate-message guard via `peer.IsDuplicatedMessage(msgId, emptyChannel)`. After safe action, if `ctx.Send` → reconstruct `ChatMessageEvent` → `SendEvent(ChatMessage)` to peer.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ClubServer\GameServer\IncomingGameServerPeer.cs` (~906 LOC — **club-server side, mirror of `OutgoingClubServerPeer`**; see `club-server` app entry for full detail). Receives 19 op-codes from game-servers, sends 3 outbound notifications (`NotifyClubServer` / `NotifyClubDisbanded` / `NotifyChampThresholdPassed`).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\ChatServer\GameServer\IncomingGameServerPeer.cs` (~495 LOC — **chat-server side, mirror of `OutgoingChatServerPeer`**; see `chat-server` app entry). 3 ops (`Authenticate` / `Debug` / `RegisterGameServer`) + 3 inbound events (`UpdateGameState` / `SendChatMessage` / `ConfirmMessageDelivery`). Chat-server transports messages but does NOT dispatch the ~40 message-type codes (`messageEvent.Data`) — that happens on the game-server side.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\GameServer\IncomingGameServerPeer.cs` (~728 LOC — **master-server side, mirror of `OutgoingMasterServerPeer`**; see `master-server` app entry). Receives `RegisterGameServer` op + 4 inbound events (`UpdateServer` / `UpdateGameState` / `RemoveGameState` / `UpdateAppStats`). Owns `MonitorLoop` heartbeat watchdog + file-based state machine (`Flags\UpdateServerStateDelay`). Three-way S2S inbound symmetry across master / chat / club is now complete.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\OutgoingClubServerPeer.cs` (~1129 LOC, **bidirectional + per-peer facade**): S2S to `club-server`. Outbound app-level: `RegisterGameServer` handshake; after Ok → `FlushLeagueClubPoints` (batched, `MaxClubPointsInChunk = 1000`, from `application.ClubPeerState`) + `application.GlobalLeaguesContext.Refresh()`; app-level club-lifecycle ops: `NotifyClubServer(LeaguesLifecycleEvent, seasonId, champId)`, `NotifyClubDisbanded(clubId)`, `NotifyPlayerBanned(playerId, bool)`, `NotifyPlayerCpRemoval(playerId)`, `DebugClubServer(DebugClubServerEvent)`; each has matching `HandleXxxResponse`. **Inbound op-request handlers** (club → game): `HandleNotifyClubServerOperation` → `application.NotifyClubServer`, `HandleNotifyClubDisbandedOperation` → `application.NotifyClubDisbanded`, `HandleNotifyChampThresholdPassed` → `application.OnChampThresholdPassed`. **Per-peer façade** — inner sealed class `ClubS2SFacade` (~L643-1112) retrieved via `GetFacadeForPeer(IGenericPeer)` (called by `GameClientPeer_Leagues`); stamps every request with `peerIndex + peerUserId` so that `GetFacadeForResponse` (L625) can route responses back via `application.Peers.FindPeer()` and invoke per-facade callbacks. **7 facade operations** (each with `On{Xxx}` success + `On{Xxx}Failed` public event callbacks): `CreateLeagueClubPoint` (buffers into `application.ClubPeerState` when disconnected), `IncreaseCheatRating`, `GetCurrentClubStanding`, `GetStandingInSeason`, `GetStandingInChamp(seasonId, champId, divisionId?)`, `GetClubStandingInSeason(seasonId, clubId)`, `GetClubStandingInChamp(seasonId, champId, clubId)`. All facade ops early-return `-2` errorCode when `LeaguesAdapter.IsLeaguesOn = false` — callers can't distinguish "disabled" vs "network fail". Inner sealed class `State` (~L572-615) — thread-safe (`lockObject`) auto-incrementing EntityId list of pending `LeagueClubPoint`, `AddClubPoint`/`RemoveClubPoint`/`ToList`/`Count`; orphan-risk: if flush response is lost, `IsSentToService` already set true → retry path missing.

- `monetization` **(system)** — **real-money** payments only. Contains `prem-shop` (sells "products" for real money — product packs, in-game currency, licenses, pond passes) and `product-delivery` (delivers products bought offline). Not to be confused with `economy` (in-game currency).

- `economy` **(system)** — tentative name. In-game currency + in-game items/licenses traded for that currency. Contains `shop`. Name uncertain — see section L.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Balance\BalanceHelper.cs` (~226 LOC — **currency-wallet primitive used by dozens of call-sites across GameLogic**: purchases / missions / bonuses / fishing sessions / tournaments / clubs / leaderboards / reel-of-fortune / etc.). Sync API: `IncrementBalance(profile, currency, value, BalanceMovementType, message, preventNegative=false)` + `LogBalanceIncrement` (log-only if already incremented). Async API: `IncrementBalanceAsync` (logging fires async via `action.AsyncInvoke`) + `LogBalanceIncrementAsync`. Validation: `Check(profile, currency, cost)` boolean can-afford. Implementation: `preventNegativeBalance` flag clamps debits to available balance; two-table-write per op (statement via `Logger.Stmt` + analytics `BalanceDto`). `BalanceMovementType` enum (BonusFromProduct/BonusFromMission/Transfer/Purchase/...). **Dangerous**: analytics logging failures silently caught (~L201-207, every ~100th error logged; TODO in code).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Monetization.cs` (method: `HandleExchangeCurrency` — Gold↔Silver swap via `BalanceHelper.IncrementBalance` with anti-cheat gate and `LogCurrencyExchange` analytics)
- `shop` — in-game shop: player buys **inventory items** and **licenses** (pond access) with in-game currency (SC/credits or GC/baitcoins). Part of `economy` system. Not to be confused with `prem-shop` (real money). Licenses overlap with `travel` module — see section L.
  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Shop\` (~23 files ~439 LOC — `IShopProvider`: `GetAllItems` / `GetAllItemsTable` / `GetLicenses` / `GetInventoryParams` / `UpdateInventoryItemParams` / `GetTargetedAds`; DTOs `InventoryItemDto` / `InventoryParamDto` / `LicenseDto` / `BrandDto` / `CategoryItemCount` / `ItemCategoryDto` / `LoyaltyBonusDto`; **TYPO `LincenseTranslationDto`** with public fields instead of properties; dispersed across `shop` + `prem-shop` + `inventory-items` + `licenses`)

  - `Shared\SharedLib\Shop\` (6 files ~236 LOC — **item-template rendering subsystem**): `MultilingualTemplate.cs` extends `Dict<int, string>` lang→template + `ParsedParamNames[]` + `Parameters{}` for substitution; `InventoryParam.cs` DTO hierarchy (`id/category/name/unit/values` + extended variant with `ExtendedValueContainer`); **`InventoryParamProducer.cs`** — **template engine** for item descriptions: given `InventoryItem`+`categoryId`+`languageId`+`ItemParameterTemplateData`, looks up template, extracts `{paramName}` tokens, resolves typed values (string/float), converts (Enum→localized / Measurement metric↔imperial for lang=1 USA: m→ft, kg→lbs / None passthrough), substitutes back; `InventorySortingGroup.cs` UI hierarchy model (`Id`/`ParentId?`/`Name`/`Order`/`Icon`/`HintElementId` tree); `ItemParameterTemplateData.cs` config container (dict category → language-indexed templates + measurement-unit translations); `MeasurementUnits.cs` enum (None/Enum/Meter/Centimeter/Milimeter/Kilogram/Gram).

- `prem-shop` — premium shop: sells "products" (item packs, in-game currency, licenses, pond passes) for **real money**. Part of `monetization` system. Catalog, product lookup with platform-specific price overrides (Steam DLC via `SteamHelper`), PlayStation composite-product expansion (recursive inner-product resolution with premium multiplier merging), region-specific hacks (Retail PS), offers/sales, in-game-currency sub-purchase flow.

- `inventory` **(system)** — separate large system (not part of `economy`). Contains `inventory-items` (core), `wear` (deterioration), `rod-setup` (tackle presets), `repair` (durability restoration).

- `repair` — item durability restoration. Two flows: (1) money-based via shop — `HandleRepairOperation` (84 LOC, multi-item preview + cost aggregation + balance deduction + analytics); (2) kit-based via `repair kits` consumable — `UseRepairKits` (94 LOC, validation, rod-slot state via processor, batch repair + kit deduction). Anti-cheat: `RepairOnPond` (illegal), `NoItemToRepair`. Part of `inventory` system.
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Inventory\Tools\` (3 files ~54 LOC: Spoon + Thermometer + FishScaler)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Inventory.cs` (methods: `HandleRepairOperation`, `UseRepairKits`)
- `gifting` — gift creation, transmission (via ChatServer), and receipt. Sender creates gift via `MakeGift` (delegates anti-cheat + item decrement to `InventoryAdapter.MakeGift`), then `SendGift` wraps the item + count + receiver into a chat message. Receiver's `ProcessGift` handler unpacks and adds to inventory. Standalone module; touches `inventory-items`, `messaging`, `anti-cheat`.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Inventory.cs` (3 methods / 74 LOC: `MakeGift` (delegates to InventoryAdapter), `SendGift`, `ProcessGift`)
- `inventory-items` — core inventory management: fish-cage marking, consumption (with firework branch → bridges to `fish-generator`), gifting, asset delivery, obfuscation (strips server-only properties before sending to client), disassembly, in-hand tool selection (Firework / Chum / Catapult). Part of `inventory` system. Heavy anti-cheat coupling (10+ calls).
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Inventory\Main\` (12 files ~1.6k LOC — `Inventory` class extends List<InventoryItem> + `InventoryItem` base + `InventoryChange`; **`Inventory_Can.cs` throws `NotImplementedException` for unknown storage types** ~L267)
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Inventory\Misc\` (6 files ~156 LOC misc catch gear)
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Inventory\Property\` (5 files ~130 LOC fish house / trophy room)
  - `Shared\Photon.Interfaces\Inventory\` (2 files ~34 LOC — `InventoryOperationCode` + `InventoryErrorCode` + `InventoryParameterCode` 22 keys ItemId/ItemStorage/ItemParent/ItemCount/ItemSlot/ItemUpdates)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\DalAdapters\InventoryAdapter.cs` (minus `GenerateDailyWear` → wear; minus `HandleFishGenerationEvent` + firework path → fish-generator bridge)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeerExtensions.cs` (inventory transaction helpers: `DoInventoryTransaction`, `DoInventoryTransactionEvent`, `DoInventoryTransactionManualEvent`, `OnInventoryChange`, `OnMoveRelated`, `SendItemsUpdatedToClient` (2 overloads), `PopulateParameters` (inventory changes → response))
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Inventory.cs` (primary 137 KB partial — 28 `InventoryOperationCode` dispatcher + item manipulation: `HandleInventoryOperation` (81 LOC dispatch), Move/Split/Combine/Subordinate/Replace/SplitAndReplace/SwapRods item mutations, `ConsumeItem`/`MakeGift` delegates, `SetLeaderLength`/`SetShimCount`/`HandleSetClipLength` tackle tweaks, `HandleTakeToolItem` (player-tools absorbed here), `PublishPropertiesChangedEvent`, `TryCompensateRodCantBeModifiedWhenCasted`, `ProcessInventoryChange/MoveRelatedItem/LoseItem`, `UpdateRodInGameEngine` (56 LOC mostly `game-state` bridge))
- `product-delivery` — delivers products that users bought offline (Steam DLC ownership, refund detection, Android offline refund handling, transaction logging; logs IAP transaction facts with payment system / USD price / region). Part of `monetization` system. **Partially woven into** `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Auth\LoginAdapter.cs` (shared file with `auth` module — a codebase-wide pattern of intertwined code).
  - `Shared\Epic\EpicHelper.cs` (ownership verification — but **`ValidateOwnershipToken()` throws `NotImplementedException` L325** with message "unsafe without validating entitlement token" — incomplete feature)
  - `Shared\Nintendo\NintendoHelper.cs` (Nintendo eShop entitlement-confirmation post-purchase delivery)
  - `Shared\XblRestApi\XblApiHelper\XblApi.cs` (Xbox Live REST calls to entitlements API via delegated-auth — cross-cuts with `auth`)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\ProductDeliveryService.cs` (~125 LOC — **routing entry-point** for all purchase-delivery modules): `DeliverProduct` (online) / `DeliverProductOffline` (load → deliver → save for absent players) / `DeliverPendingItems` (on-login catch-up returning new + retry product-IDs) / `CreateDeliveryItems` (master-server audit-only, no delivery when player offline) / `RecordRefund` (mark items refunded). Router dispatches to **tracked (new) vs direct (legacy)** delivery based on `EnvironmentVariableCache.UseTrackedDelivery` env flag — **toggling mid-production risks partial-delivery inconsistency** (tracked DB vs live profile).
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\TrackedProductDelivery.cs` (**~980 LOC — the delivery engine**): auditable delivery with **8 component types** (currency / subscription / pond-unlocks / items / licenses / inventory-extensions / skins / rod-setups); `BuildDeliveryItems` creates audit rows; `DeliverComponent` dispatches to 8 per-component handlers; `DeliverPendingItems` resilient retry with **per-failed-item isolation** (creates retry-record + continues). **`DeliverPondUnlocks` god** handles PlayStation compensation-pass dupe-pond logic (~L529-545 special-case `[pondId, pondId]` → `DeliverCompensationPondPass`), permanent vs temporary unlocks, existing-pass extension vs new-pass creation. `DeliverInventoryExtensions` refreshes capacity + per-slot-type logging.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\DeliveryContent.cs` (7 typed DTOs for JSON serialization in delivery tracking: `CurrencyDeliveryContent` / `SubscriptionDeliveryContent` / `PondUnlocksDeliveryContent` / `ItemsDeliveryContent` / `LicensesDeliveryContent` / `InventoryExtensionsDeliveryContent` / `SkinsDeliveryContent`)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\MonetizationHelper.cs` (~595 LOC — **shared monetization utilities** used by all delivery/purchase paths): `GetLicenseRefs`/`GetItemBriefs`/`GetSkinElements` JSON-array deserializers; **`FromDto(ProductDto)` transforms product DTO → `ProfileProduct`** (loads items/licenses/rod-setups from cache, generates instance IDs); `BuildInventoryItems` complex hydration with nested items + rod-setup reconstruction; **`ReplaceBundleTransactions`/`ReplaceBundleTransactionFacts`** — analytics detect consequent txs within **5s window as bundle purchases** (50%+ match threshold, hardcoded); `PopulateTransactionPrice`/`SaveClientTransaction` with fallback to similar-txs for regional pricing; `TryGetEquivalentPrice` USD-normalization via exchange-rate + platform-fee %.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Web\ProductHelper.cs` (~705 LOC — **admin/web-side product delivery orchestrator**): `SendProductToPlayer` offline-message dispatch via `PhotonHelper.RunOnMaster`; `GiveOfflineProduct` applies `ProfileProduct` to profile + triggers notifier callback; `DeliverInitialStarters` distributes starter kits by platform/region; `PutProductToProfileAndLog` core delivery with balance logging; ~15 sub-loggers (`LogMoneyDelivery`/`LogProductLicensesDelivery`/`LogPondUnlocksDelivery`/`LogInventoryExtDelivery`/`LogProductSkinElementsDelivery`/`LogSubscriptionUpdated`/`LogLicenseChanged` etc.); **`RefundProduct`** multi-system reversal (items / licenses / subscriptions / extensions / pond unlocks / skin elements / balance), each sub-system tracks own logs (`DalFactory.GetLogger().Trade/Inventory`).
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Web\EntityCloningRule.cs` (~24 LOC WebAdmin bulk-entity cloning DTO — `OriginalId int?` / `OriginalGuid Guid?` / `SharedTranslatedFields string[]` for linked translations; used in admin UI for template cloning)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Web\TranStatuses.cs` (~12 LOC transaction-status constants — `StatusNew`/`StatusComplete`/`StatusCanceled`/`StatusFailed`/`StatusRefunded`/`StatusRemoved`)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Game\DistributedCache.cs` (~27 LOC static wrapper around `DalFactory.GetDistributedDataProvider()` — `TryPutDataToCache(key, data)` + `GetDataFromCache(key)` / `<T>` with JSON serialization; cross-cutting infra)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Auth\LoginAdapter.cs` (parts — see `auth` module entry)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\DalAdapters\AnalyticsAdapter.cs` (methods: `LogTransactionFact` 2 overloads — IAP transaction facts)

- `cache` — caching module; note: folder is named `Caching` but the module name is `cache` (historical misnaming). Core lives in `Shared\SharedLib\Caching\` (infra) + `Shared\SharedLib\Config\` (56 domain cache classes, ~10k LOC) organized in 3 dependency tiers. L0 tier (independent): AbTest / Clubs / EnvironmentVariable / GlobalVariables / JsonVariables (+2 partials) / Eula / FishingTogether / GameServer (PondIds) / InitialProfile / InventorySortingGroups / ItemCategory / License / LoyaltyBonus / Object / PushNotifications / SaltwaterWearPenalty / States / Skins / TargetedAds / Tournaments / TournamentHistory / TranslationTerms / UsernameParts / Weather / DailyMissions / AbTest / PlatformMapping / ItemFishAttraction / StatesCache. L1 tier (depends on L0): Event / Item / ItemAsset / Monetization / Rewards / Fortune / Tops / DailyMissions / Targeted Ads. L2 tier (depends on L1): Achievements / BiteSystem / Fortune / Leveling / Leagues / Leaderboards (3 partials Competitive/Fish/Global) / Mission / ThirdPartyAds / TournamentHistory. **Infra files** (not domain caches): `CacheClasses.cs` (generic hash wrappers `EntityHash<T>`/`PondHash<T>`/`NameHash<T>`/`DateHash<T>`/`LanguageHash<T>`/`PlatformHash<T>` + `IEntityHash<K,T>`), `CacheGroups.cs` (enum: DT/AbTests/Variables/Localization/InitialProfile/Rewards etc.), `ConfigParametersProvider.cs` (DAL adapter — connection strings + AppSettings), `ConfigurationException.cs`, `ServerConstants.cs` (keystore path + push defaults — see private audit), `StaticHandlersConfig.cs` (S2S handler registration bootstrap — ItemFactory / LicenseFactory / AbTestSelection / MissionContext init), `TaskParallelUtility.cs` (parallel task loader with exception aggregation), `JsonVariablesCache.cs` + `_DailyMissions` / `_MergedLog` partials (JSON-blob config loader). **Dispersal**: each domain cache conceptually belongs to its module (`ItemCache` → `inventory-items`, `MonetizationCache` → `shop`/`prem-shop`, `AchievementsCache` → `achievements`, etc.) — Pass 2 module cards should grep review for `XxxCache` to assemble. Key cross-cutting caches: **`ItemCache`** (consumed by `inventory-items`/`shop`/`prem-shop`/`rewards`/`missions`/`leaderboards`/`daily-missions`/`events`/`bite-system`/all item-using modules), **`GlobalVariablesCache`** (injection-point for 40+ static fields across `game-state`/`inventory-items`/`chum`/`physics-model`/`bite-system`/`leaderboards`/`together`/`ads`), **`RewardsCache`** (`rewards`/`levels`/`leaderboards`/`tournaments`/`missions`/`achievements`), **`EnvironmentVariableCache`** (`leaderboards`/`together`/diagnostics), **`TranslationTermsCache`** (`localization` + all modules with user-facing strings), **`AbTestCache`** (`ads`/`progression`/`missions` feature-flagging), **`PlatformMapping`** (all platform-scoped code). **Module-specific** (low cross-cutting): `MissionCache`/`DailyMissionsCache`/`AchievementsCache`/`FortuneCache`/`FishingTogetherCache`/`TargetedAdsCache`/`ThirdPartyAdsCache` (deprecated)/`TopsCache` (legacy). **Notable god-caches**: `ItemCache.cs` (910 LOC — multilingual items + local shop overrides + boats + inventory images), `GameServerCache.cs` (902 LOC — pond IDs / carousel / visible ponds / locations), `MonetizationCache.cs` (774 LOC — currencies/products/offers/subscriptions/platform fees/pond unlocks), `TournamentsCache.cs` (752 LOC), `GlobalVariablesCache.cs` (687 LOC), `MissionCache.cs` (633 LOC — version-counter on refresh for client change-detection).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameApplication.cs` (**cache-init cascade & refresh-signal coordination** — 3 dependency levels: L0 independent (~20 caches: `AbTestCache`, `ClubsCache`, `EnvironmentVariableCache`, `GlobalVariablesCache`, `JsonVariablesCache`, `EulaCache`, `FishCache`, `FishingTogetherCache`, `GameServerCache.InitializePondIdsDefault`, `InitialProfileCache`, `InventorySortingGroupsCache`, `ItemCategoryCache`, `LicenseCache`, `LoyaltyBonusCache`, `ObjectCache`, `PushNotificationsCache`, `SaltwaterWearPenaltyCache`, `StatesCache`, `SkinsCache`, `TargetedAdsCache`, `TournamentsCache`, `TournamentHistoryCache`, `TranslationTermsCache`, `UsernamePartsCache`, `WeatherCache`, `DailyMissionsCache`); L1 depend-on-L0 (`EventCache`, `GameServerCache.Initialize`, `ItemCache`, `ItemAssetCache`, `MonetizationCache`, `RewardsCache`); L2 depend-on-L1 (`AchievementsCache`, `BiteSystemCache.InitOnGame`, `FortuneCache`, `LevelingCache`, `LeaguesCache`, `LeaderboardsCache`, `MissionCache`, `ThirdPartyAdsCache`). Refresh-signal subscribers on `Caches.OnRefreshDone` (all check `if (caches == null || caches.Contains(CacheName))` filter): `InjectGlobalVariablesIntoGameEngine` (~36 LOC — FishEscapeModel / Game disconnect timeouts / GameProcessor / Lure / LeaderCutters / LineBreaker static refresh), `InjectGlobalVariablesIntoBiteSystem` (~18 LOC — FishSelector probabilities/distance), `InjectGlobalVariablesIntoClubActivityModel` (~12 LOC — club-activity reward multipliers), `InjectGlobalVariablesIntoAntiCheatFishingManager` (~12 LOC — landing-net thresholds), `InjectGlobalVariablesIntoPeer` (~8 LOC — TPM ping thresholds), `InjectEnvVariablesIntoFishStatsAdapter` (~7 LOC), `NotifyClientsAboutFortuneCachesRefreshed` (~10 LOC — reel-of-fortune context sync), `NotifyPeersAboutAchievementCachesRefreshed` (~10 LOC — per-peer AM reinit + check), `NotifyPeersAboutBitesystemCacheRefreshed` (~10 LOC — per-peer processor bite-map reinit), `NotifyClientsAboutCachesRefreshed` (~28 LOC — selective broadcast of GlobalVars/Tournaments/Licenses/Leaderboards compressed JSON); plus `EventCache.ActiveEventChanged += NotifyClientsAboutActiveEventChanged` (~20 LOC — per-language obfuscated active-event broadcast). `CacheRefreshHelper.Start` (with dev-server shorter timeout via `SharedConsts.CacheRefreshTimeoutOnDev` unless `NotUpdatableCache`) / `Stop` on TearDown. `DataCache.ExceptionHandler` routes cache-load exceptions → `DiagAdapter.SaveServerError` + `AnalyticsAdapter.SaveGameException`.)

  - `Shared\SharedLib\Config\` (~56 files, ~10k LOC — see module-overview text above for complete tier + dispersal breakdown)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Helpers\` (12 files ~1.4k LOC — **pure cross-cutting utilities, no single module owner**): `UnitOfWork.cs` (**296 LOC transaction/saga pattern base**, `class UnitOfWork<S, A> : IUnitOfWork where S : Enum, A : ISharedLibAdapter` — lifecycle `Initialize`/`ExecuteResult`/`SafeExecute` wrapping with try-catch/timing/log; 3 status-streams `VerboseStatus`/`SuccessStatus`/`FailureStatus`; parent-chaining via `SetParent(parentWork)` to bubble status up; Mongo logging hooks; `RethrowException` default-false = **silent failures** unless caller checks `StatusCode`. Heavily used in `leagues` module — 11 `Shared\SharedLib\Leagues\UnitOfWork_*.cs` files derive from this); `ParameterDictionaryExtensions.cs` (260 LOC — Photon byte-keyed param-dict encode/decode for 15+ types incl. int/long/Guid/DateTime/JSON/compressed-JSON; **all peer-to-peer communication uses this**); `StringDictionaryExtensions.cs` (163 LOC string-keyed variant for HTTP / config); `VariablesDictionary.cs` (130 LOC typed config-container with bool/int/float/DateTime/enum/JSON getters + log on default-fallback); `DataFileHelper.cs` (95 LOC CSV/GZip bulk-import parser); `Rational.cs` (80 LOC immutable exact-fraction struct — no float-loss probabilities / drop rates / bids; `checked` arithmetic; safe to ~10^9); `ExceptionExtensions.cs` (55 LOC — `GetMessageWithInner` / `GetStackTraceWithInner` deep-chain formatters for logging); `IpAddressHelper.cs` (55 LOC — IP parsing + version detection + local-IP resolution); `TextHelper.cs` (47 LOC — range-string parser `"1-5,7,9-10" → [1,2,3,4,5,7,9,10]`); `MathUtility.cs` (31 LOC — `Lerp`/`Clamp` with `[MethodImpl(AggressiveInlining)]` hot-path); `EnumerableExtensions.cs` (26 LOC — nullable-struct aggregate with default fallback); `PingPongTraversalIterator.cs` (200 LOC — niche alternate-left/right iterator from array ends, used for spatial proximity or fairness scheduling).

- `disconnect` — graceful disconnect signaling and propagation across servers (reads signals from DAL, propagates to connected peers); also fact-logging of disconnect events (reason codes, RTT metrics, client IP, room); and the per-peer disconnect lifecycle (PreviewDisconnect → OnDisconnect → DoDisconnect with cleanup). Multiple concerns — "signal delivery" vs "disconnect facts" vs "lifecycle" — see section L.

- `game` **(system)** — tangled umbrella over `game-actions`, `game-state`, `fish-fight`, `game-model-core`, and likely more `game-*` modules; boundaries blurry, full of bugs — main target of this KB-mapping effort. All `game-*` assignments are tentative.
- `game-state` — state-machine for in-game transitions (throw, reel, pause/resume, finish-move, leave-location, reset, …); raises `InvalidTransition` on illegal transitions; ping-driven "need client reset" emission for stale transitions; ignore-transition counters to tolerate client duplicates. Also includes scene-seed management (random seed for scene reproducibility, with main/temp switching on tournament/FT sessions similar to fishing-session). Tentative — boundary with `game-actions` and `game-model-core` still blurry.
  - `Shared\Photon.Interfaces\Game\` (3 files ~80 LOC: `GameActionCode` enum 25 actions Throw/Water/Spool/Move/FightFish/CatchFish/Board/Walk + `GameActionCodeExtensions.IsAllowedOnPause()` + `BaitConsumeReason` + `FishEscapeStatus`)

  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\GameStates.cs` (states enum)

  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\SceneStateManager.cs` (scene-seed init/reset/switch; per-session determinism)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\GameProcessor.cs` (**5867 LOC** — per-rod fishing-cycle driver: cast → move → bite → fight → catch; state-machine subscriber; anti-cheat integration; ~32 cross-module touchpoints; 12 god-methods >100 LOC; primary home here but DISPERSED across many modules via sub-engines below. Leak to `licenses`: `HandleAttackFinished` / `HandleCatchFish` do license checks — belong to `licenses` module conceptually)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\MultiRodGameProcessor.cs` (70 KB — orchestrates up to 5 rods; routes actions per-slot; owns shared state that spans rods)

  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\` (8 files ~2.7k LOC — **core `leaderboards` implementation**, 3×2 structure: `LeaderboardsAdapter` main + 3 sub-domain partials × `LeaderboardsHelper` main + 3 sub-domain partials). **Adapter = stateful orchestration** (holds `ILeaderboardsProvider` DAL + `ILogBase` logger, lazy `CreateLeaguesAdapter` for club-points integration, executes DB writes + reward distribution). **Helper = pure stateless logic** (DTO ↔ domain conversions, dimension-field-name mappings, analytics message parsing — no DAL calls).

  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsAdapter_Competitive.cs` (~735 LOC): 19 methods organized by category — **Status** (Initialize/Get/Set `LeaderboardProcessingStatus` 8-state machine: Unknown → Upcoming → Current → Passed → HistorySaved → Processing → Processed → Cleaning → Cleaned); **Updates** (`UpdateCompetitiveLeaderboards(TournamentKinds, TournamentIndividualResultsDto[])` called from `TournamentEndAdapter` — increments CompetitionsPlayed/Won/Rating across all 3 periods simultaneously, role-filtered to None/Insider/Moderator; `Admin` variants for manual corrections); **Retrieval** (`GetCompetitiveLeaderboards` 3 query-modes `Top100AndUserAndSurrounding` default / `Top100` / `Top100AndUser`); **Processing pipeline** (`RotateCurrentCompetitiveLeaderboards` status transitions; `FinalizeCompetitiveLeaderboard` finalization + reward distribution; `CalculateCompetitiveLeaderboardChange`; `CleanupCompetitiveLeaderboardsData` batched delete loop; `DistributeLeaderboardRewards<T>` generic reward sender); **Feature flags** 5 static (`IsCompetitiveLeaderboardsUpdateOn`/`RewardsOn`/`JobsOn`/`UIOn`/`QueryType`). Reward flow: period ends → status `Passed` → `SaveCompetitiveLeaderboardHistory` → `DistributeLeaderboardRewards` loads reward from `LeaderboardsCache.CompetitiveLeaderboardRewards` by (TournamentKind, DimensionType, PeriodType, Place) → `reward.CloneReward` + loot-table `RewardUtils.SelectSpecificReward(rnd.NextDouble(), reward)` → `SendChatMessagesReliable(ChatRequests.CompetitiveLeaderboardsResult)` async. **Club points integration** (~L672-708): winners get optional club-points via `LeaguesAdapter.GetPlayersEligibleForClubPointReward` + `AdminGiveClubPointsBulk(source=LeagueClubPointSources.Leaderboard)` — fire-and-forget with `onSuccess/onFailure` callbacks. Dimensions mapped only for `TournamentKinds.Competition` (Played/Won/Rating) — other kinds unsupported.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsAdapter_Fish.cs` (~772 LOC): per-pond × per-species ranking by Weight. `GetPondFish(pondId, languageId)` + `GetPondFishForms(pondId, fishCodeName, languageId)` + `GetFishLeaderboardSpecies(languageId)` enumerates `FishLeaderboardSpecie(CodeName, Id, Name, PondIds[])` via `BiteSystemCache.GetGrouppedFishListFormFromMaps` + `FishCache.GetFishBrief` + `GameServerCache.ActivePondIds`. `UpdateFishLeaderboards(Profile, pondId, fishCodeName, fishId, weight, source)` validates `source ∈ FishLeaderboardsAcceptedFishSources` (static string[] config — silent-reject if unset). Same processing pipeline as Competitive but keyed on (PondId, FishCodeName, PeriodType). `ChatRequests.FishLeaderboardsResult` delivery. **Combinatorial explosion concern**: 20 ponds × 50 species × 3 periods = 3000 leaderboards.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsAdapter_Global.cs` (~715 LOC): lifetime XP + 5 fish-counter rankings. 6 independent dimensions: `Experience` (cumulative player XP = Experience + RankExperience) + `YoungFish`/`CommonFish`/`TrophyFish`/`UniqueFish`/`TotalFish` counters. `UpdateGlobalLeaderboards(Profile, experienceIncrement?, youngFish?, commonFish?, trophyFish?, uniqueFish?, totalFish?, source?)` accepts per-dimension increments; if `totalFishIncrement > 0`, source must be in `FishLeaderboardsAcceptedFishSources`. `ChatRequests.GlobalLeaderboardsResult`. Same processing pipeline + club points flow.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsHelper.cs` (~75 LOC main — static partial): DTO ↔ domain converters `LeaderboardPeriod FromDto/ToDto` + `LeaderboardStanding FromDto` + `InitHistory<T>` (sets FinalDate = period-end - 1 day, PeriodName e.g. "Year 2024 Week 15") + `NullOrEquals` filter helpers.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsHelper_Competitive.cs` (~160 LOC): `CompetitiveLeaderboardPeriod` ↔ DTO; `CompetitiveLeaderboardReward`/`Standing`/`History` FromDto; **`GetDimensionFieldName(TournamentKind, DimensionType)`** → DB field name via `CompetitiveActivityDimensionFieldNameMapping` (**only `TournamentKinds.Competition` mapped** — future tournament kinds need schema + mapping update); `GetSupportedTournamentKinds()` yields Competition only; `ToDictionary(LeaderboardResultMessage<CompetitiveLeaderboardPeriod>)` for analytics + `ParseCompetitiveLeaderboardResultMessage` reverse.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsHelper_Fish.cs` (~89 LOC): `FishLeaderboardPeriod` ↔ DTO + Reward + History converters + analytics message parser. No dimension mapping (single ranking per pond/species).
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leaderboards\LeaderboardsHelper_Global.cs` (~143 LOC): `GlobalLeaderboardPeriod` ↔ DTO + Standing + History + `GlobalActivityDimensionFieldNameMapping` (Experience/YoungFish/CommonFish/TrophyFish/UniqueFish/TotalFish) + message serialization. Commented-out `// Experience = dto.Experience,` (~L53) but uncommented 2 lines later — likely merge conflict / incomplete refactor.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Leaderboards.cs` (372 LOC): `LeaderboardsAdapter` lazy init; **`HandleLeaderboardOperation` (58 LOC)** dispatcher — 7 sub-ops: `GetCompetitiveLeaderboardRewards`/`GetCompetitiveLeaderboards`/`GetGlobalLeaderboardRewards`/`GetGlobalLeaderboards`/`GetFishLeaderboardRewards`/`GetFishLeaderboards`/`GetFishLeaderboardSpecies`; reward handlers clone + localize; async inbound `OnReceiveMessage_Leaderboards` → `Process{Competitive/Global/Fish}LeaderboardResult` (18-21 LOC each) → `RewardManager.SelectSpecificReward` + `RewardManager.GiveDeferredReward` with `BalanceMovementType.{Competitive/Global/Fish}LeaderboardReward` + `Profile.Stats.LeaderboardPlaceTaken` + leaderboard audit log; `TryRaiseLeaderboardsResetEvent` (22 LOC); env-flag `EnvironmentVariableCache.IsLeaderboardsOn`
- `leagues` — clubs compete in league seasons; per-season/per-championship/per-division/per-league standings; season-end & champ-end rewards; ban/unban enforcement; club-point accumulation with cheat-rating integration. Real-time standings kept by `club-server` app — this module is the **client-facing + S2S-caller side**. Distinct from `clubs` (membership) — leagues = competitive seasons.

  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leagues\GlobalLeaguesContext.cs` (~390 LOC — **game-server app-wide immutable state holder**): props `Seasons: List<LeagueSeason>` + `ActiveSeason` + `RecentSeason` (ended <N hours ago window) + `ActiveChamp` + `RecentChamp`. Single `lockObjectData` lock for all properties. `Initialize()` subscribes to `Caches.OnRefreshDone` + calls `LoadSeasonsFromCache` (clones seasons/champs from `LeaguesCache.GetSeasons + GetPopulatedChamps`, resets runtime state). **`LoadActiveSeasonAndChamp` (~121 LOC god-method)** re-syncs champ/season props from DB + loads clubs via `adapter.LoadSeasonClubs + LoadChampDivisions + LoadChampClubs` + detects changes → raises `ActiveSeasonChampChanged(SeasonChanged, ChampChanged, ClubsChanged)` event (subscribed by game-server for client broadcasts). Special case: `LeaguesLifecycleEvent.ChampReviewEnded` → reload season clubs for updated disqualification info. Events: `SeasonsReloaded`, `ActiveSeasonChampChanged`. `OnClubDisbanded(clubId)` updates club.DisbandDate in context + DB.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leagues\InMemoryClubPointService.cs` + **4 partials** (~1.5k LOC total — **real-time scoring engine living in `club-server` app**). Core data (InMemoryClubPointService.cs): `History: ConcurrentList<LeagueStandingUpdate>` (all scored points in-flight + saved), `SeasonClubStanding` / `AllChampClubStanding` / `SeasonPlayerStanding` / `AllChampPlayerStanding` (nested dicts keyed by clubId/champId/userId → score+timestamp+cheat), `ChampDivisionClubs: Dict<champId, Dict<divisionId, Set<clubId>>>`, `SeasonClubDisqualification: Set<clubId>`, `BannedPlayers: Set<userId>`, `ClubMembers: Dict<clubId, Set<userId>>`. `_API.cs` (~238 LOC — `GetClubScoreInSeason` / `GetPlayerScoreInSeason` (return 0 if wrong season / disqualified) / `GetStandingInSeason` / `GetStandingInChamp` returning `List<LeagueClub>` / `GetClubStandingInChamp` full club standing + players with cheat-rating stripped). `_Debug.cs` debug/CSV-export endpoints. `_Persistence.cs` (~479 LOC): **`CreateLeagueClubPoint` (~127 LOC god hot-path)** — validates active season/champ match + not-disqualified + not-banned, upserts season club score, upserts season player score, denormalizes `ClubMembers[clubId].Add(userId)`, if champ event: repeats for champ buckets + `ChampDivisionClubs[champId][divisionId].Add(clubId)`, populates `LeagueClubStanding + LeaguePlayerStanding` output, fires `ChampClubPointsThresholdPassed` event if score crosses `LeaguesLogic.ChampClubPointsThreshold`; `IncreaseLeagueCheatRating` (~102 LOC); `FullReload` (loads all standings + disqualifications from DB for active season/champ); `SaveToDatabase` (~35 LOC inside lock — `EliminateDuplicates` reverse-iterates History keeping first per (seasonId, champId?, clubId, userId) for idempotent dedupe → mark `IsSaving=true` → `SaveToDatabaseBulk` or `SaveToDatabaseSingleRow` → mark saved/failed). `_Thread.cs` — background flush thread wakes every 200ms; if `LastSaveTime > 5000ms (ClubServerSettings.PersistClubPointsIntervalMs)` and not paused → `SaveToDatabaseSafe`. `ConfigureActiveSeason`/`ConfigureActiveChamp` acquire `lockObjectConfig` + call Pause/SaveToDatabase/Resume.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leagues\ILeaguesPeer.cs` + `MockLeaguesPeer.cs` + `StandaloneLeaguesPeer.cs` — peer contracts: `ILeaguesPeer` expects `Profile` + `DoOnClubPeer(Action<IClubPeer>)` + event hooks. `MockLeaguesPeer` used in `GameApplication.CreateLeaguesAdapter(MockLeaguesPeer)` — **`DoOnClubPeer` returns `true` without calling action (dev/test mode silently skips S2S)**. `StandaloneLeaguesPeer` for offline-peer variant (chat-server-routed messages).
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leagues\SafeIdQueue.cs` — thread-safe ID queue (simple `List<int>` with lock) used by `TryStartSeason` / `TryStartChamp` to track season-IDs awaiting scheduled start; **no removal on thread kill** — if AppDomain unloads mid-work, ID orphaned + server restart skips it.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Leagues\UnitOfWork_*.cs` (**11 scheduled-job atomic ops**, all inherit from `Shared\SharedLib\Helpers\UnitOfWork.cs`): lifecycle flow is `TryScheduleChamps → TryStartSeason → TryStartChamp → [points accumulating] → TryEndChamp → TryEndChampReview → EndChampReview → (loop champs) → TryEndSeason → TryEndSeasonReview → EndSeasonReview → (after horizon) TryArchiveSeasons`; plus `TryUnbanPlayers` as separate periodic job. Details — `TryScheduleChamps` (template → create Season/Leagues/Champs in DB; commented-out cleanup `DeleteSeasonChamps` at ~L74 — abandoned); `TryStartSeason` (find seasons starting <5m, async Thread.Sleep poll via `Func.BeginInvoke`, `MarkSeasonStarted` + `NotifyClubServer` + broadcast to all clubs); `TryStartChamp` (similar + populate divisions/clubs); `TryEndChamp` / `TryEndSeason` (mark ended + notify); `TryEndChampReview` / `TryEndSeasonReview` (wait until `ReviewTime - InReviewPeriod` elapsed, call `EndChampReview`/`EndSeasonReview`); **`EndChampReview`** + **`EndSeasonReview`** — atomic-ish under `TransactionScope`: calculate places/rewards/trophies (→ `CalculatePlaceTrophyRewardForChamp/ForSeason` using `BalanceMovementType.LeagueChamp/LeagueSeason`) + mark disqualifications + mark repopulated + notify clubs (`ClubsNotified`/`ClubsDisqualifiedNotified`/`GroupsDisqualifiedNotified`/`ClubsRewarded`); `TryArchiveSeasons` (identify seasons past `GlobalVariablesCache.LeaguesSeasonArchivationHorizon` ~90 days → batch-move to archive tables + cache refresh); `TryUnbanPlayers` (uses CancellationTokenSource + ConcurrentDictionary queue; `Task.Delay(ct)` wait + `SetPlayerBanned(false)`).
  - (11 UnitOfWork files are **scheduled jobs triggered by `async-processor`** — `AsyncProcessor\AsyncProcessor\Jobs\Leagues\` contains 7 runners: `LeagueScheduleChampJob` / `LeagueStartSeasonJob` / `LeagueStartChampJob` / `LeagueEndSeasonJob` / `LeagueEndChampJob` / `LeagueSeasonArchivationJob` / `LeagueUnbanPlayersJob` — each wraps the corresponding `UnitOfWork_*` under `SharedLib\Leagues\`; resolved section L uncertainty)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameApplication.cs` (app-scoped leagues context + broadcast notifications): `GlobalLeaguesContext` field + `CreateLeaguesAdapter()` factory (`DalFactory.GetLeagueProvider()` + MockLeaguesPeer + `DalFactory.GetLogger().League`); `GlobalLeaguesContext.Initialize` + event subscribes `SeasonsReloaded` / `ActiveSeasonChampChanged` in `Setup()`; `NotifyClubServer(LeaguesLifecycleEvent, ...)` (~8 LOC — refresh context + broadcast to all peers' LeaguesAdapters); `NotifyClubDisbanded(int clubId)` (~3 LOC); `GlobalLeaguesContext_SeasonsReloaded` (~7 LOC — broadcast seasons-generation to all peers); `GlobalLeaguesContext_ActiveSeasonChampChanged` (~9 LOC — sync full context + request club standing on all peers); `RequestCurrentClubStanding` (~5 LOC — all-peers broadcast); `OnChampThresholdPassed(int, int)` (~8 LOC — filtered broadcast to peers in specific club)

- `missions` **(system)** — umbrella over mission-related modules. Contains: `missions` (core orchestration), `daily-missions` (scheduled regeneration), `mission-tasks` (per-task progress/tracking), `interactive-objects` (mission interaction execution). Event-driven via `MissionsManager` with 13 event handlers wired per-peer.
- `missions` (core module) — mission lifecycle (accept/start/activate/deactivate/complete/fail/restart/archive/disable-activation), mission configuration for client, mission processing loop, event routing, state restore on login, pond-specific mission time-of-day calculation, CRUD query API (GetMissionsStarted/Completed/Archived/Failed, GetActiveMission, GetMission). Part of `missions` system.

- `daily-missions` — scheduled daily-mission generation/refresh. `DailyMissionAdapter` (lazy init) + scheduler callback; end-of-day regeneration trigger; force-regenerate op. Part of `missions` system.
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\DailyMissions\` (47 files ~1k LOC — wire DTOs with nested CatchFishTasks/Entities/Enums)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\DailyMissions\` (33 files ~4k LOC — **core `daily-missions` module implementation**) organized in 6 clusters:
    - **Orchestrator** — `DailyMissionAdapter.cs` (~88 LOC main) + `_Admin.cs` (~106 LOC WebAdmin ops) + `_Core.cs` (~157 LOC context lifecycle): `GetCurrentMissions` iterator + `FindMission` + `GetNextGenerationTime` (debug-aware) + `TryGenerateMissions` (condition-check → `GenerateAllMissions` or `TryGenerateMissingMissions`) + **`GenerateAllMissions` (~77 LOC)** (moves current→recent, adjusts difficulty, calls Generator, integrates MissionsManager) + **`RegenerateMission(kind)` (~147 LOC god)** user-triggered (validate + generate + price + regen-count) + `TryGenerateMissingMissions` (~85 LOC — fill in new kinds on level-up) + `AdminRegenerateAllMissions` / `AdminClearAllMission` / `AdminRegenerateMission(id)` (~43 LOC) + `LogGeneratedMissions` (~45 LOC) + `CleanupRecentCollections` (prune recent ponds/fish/missions by age). Integrates with game-server's `MissionsManager.Container_RefreshDailyMissions`.
    - **Generator** — `DailyMissionGenerator.cs` main (~72 LOC `GenerateMissions(context)` + `GenerateMission(kind, context)` + `ExecuteWithRandom` + `IsLevelSufficient` with A/B-test gate for min-level missions) + 3 partials: `_MissionDifficulty` (~107 LOC — `AdjustCurrentMissionDifficulty` examines last-N completed/failed per kind → raise/lower tier E/EM/M/MH/H; `GetCurrentMissionDifficulty`) / `_Similarity` (~91 LOC — `GetMissionsToCheckSimilarity` pool of recent+current + `GenerateUniqueTask` retry-loop + `HasSimilarTask` scan by conditions) / `_Utils` (~80 LOC — `GetCategoryFishIds`/`GetFishId` (Young/Trophy/Unique/Common map) + `GetWeightRange`/`GetLengthRange` enum extractors + `GetSelectionWeight` matrix picker). Config source: `JsonVariablesCache.DailyMissions.GenerationSettings` (mission kinds Common/Club/Premium + dailies per kind + difficulty tiers + reward multipliers).
    - **Builders** — `MissionBuilderBase.cs` (~42 LOC template: difficulty + task-gen loop), `MissionBuilderCatch.cs` (~30 LOC dispatcher to TaskBuilder First/Second/Third), `PondPoolBuilder.cs` (~94 LOC — diversified pond set algo: recent-fish ponds + recent-visited ponds + random fill → `HashSet<int>` used across all 3 task builders).
    - **Localization & conversion** — `DailyMissionLocalizer.cs` (~35 LOC — name/description + dispatch to TaskLocalizer); **`DailyMissionUtils.cs` (~509 LOC massive converter)** — `BindContextToProfile` (populates ProfileContext lambdas level/language/ponds/club/premium), **`ConvertToMission` (DailyMission → Mission DTO + Club/Premium lock tasks + conditions wrap)**, **`CreateTaskConditionCatch`** (builds mission-condition tree from `DailyMissionTaskCatch` — pond + category + weight/length ranges + bait/lure + tackle + drag + time + place), `GetItemRequirementCategory` (item ID → `MissionRequirementBaitLure`); `ObjectModelExtensions.cs` (~23 LOC `FishStatus` ↔ `MissionRequirementFishForm`).
    - **Peer abstraction** — `IDailyMissionPeer.cs` contract (`Profile` / `LogMissionFact` / `NotifyClientAboutBalanceChange`); `MockDailyMissionPeer.cs` (24 LOC test); `StandaloneDailyMissionPeer.cs` (40 LOC WebAdmin offline — logs to DAL + silent balance notifs).
    - **`CatchFishTasks\` sub-subsystem (17 files)** — task-generation specialization for catch-fish missions, arguably a sub-module of `daily-missions`:
      - **5 cached settings services + 5 interfaces (DI pattern, singletons via `public static Shared { get; }`)**: `CachedCatchFishTaskSettingsService` ↔ `ICatchFishTaskSettings` (pond selection + rank1/2/3 condition pools + fish form/count/weight/length + bait/tackle/drag/time/place selections); `CachedPondSettingsService` ↔ `IPondSettingsService` (pond list + fish-by-category + catchability filter tackle-vs-fish-force); `CachedFishSettingsService` ↔ `IFishSettingsService` (fish entity subset); `CachedGenerationSettingsService` ↔ `IGenerationSettingsService` (generation + pond-fish weight/length row tables); `CachedTermTranslationService` ↔ `ITermTranslationService` (fish-form/condition-name translations).
      - **3 concrete TaskBuilders (NOT difficulty tiers — fishing EXPLORATION STRATEGIES)**: `TaskBuilderFirst` ("familiar waters": recent fish + recent ponds, 1:1 difficulty mapping) / `TaskBuilderSecond` ("explore known ponds": recent ponds + new fish, randomized difficulty mapping) / `TaskBuilderThird` ("go explore": random ponds + new fish, compressed difficulty mapping EasyMedium/Medium→Medium + MediumHard/Hard→Hard).
      - **`TaskBuilderBase` + 2 partials (~800 LOC)**: main abstract base (`BuildTask` orchestrator + abstract `GetTaskDifficulty` / `GetTaskConditions` + `GetAdditionalConditions` rank1/2/3 random + `InitConditionArguments`); `_FishFormCountWeight` (form/count/weight/length); `_OtherConditions` (bait-lure/tackle/drag/time/place).
      - `TaskLocalizer.cs` (~99 LOC — `DailyMissionTaskCatch` → user-readable using `ITermTranslationService` + `MeasuringSystemManager` unit localization).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_DailyMissions.cs` (entire file — 28 LOC — `IDailyMissionPeer` interface impl: `Profile` property + `LogMissionFact` → `analytics.LogMissionData`; lazy `DailyMissionAdapter` property)

Sold in `shop` (in-game currency) and `prem-shop` (real money), queried by `ponds`/`travel`. Cross-cutting — see section L.

Constructor: `(columnCount=10, columnPrefix="C")` → generates `C0..C9` columns, creates in-memory SQLite, prepares parameterized INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE. **`FindMatch(query)` / `FindMatches(query, limit)` / `FindMatchesWithValues(query, limit)` — raw SQL query composition** (see private audit). `AddColumn` / `DropColumn` (via backup-table dance due to SQLite limitation). Hardcoded 10-column cap + no property-name → column-index mapping (caller's responsibility).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\LinkedListDictionary.cs` (~147 LOC — hybrid intrusive data structure: `LinkedList<TValue>` + `Dictionary<TKey, LinkedListNode<TValue>>`. Purpose: O(1) add/remove/lookup by key + insertion-order iteration + direct-node reference for round-robin advancement (`nextJoinRandomStartNode.Next`). `Add` / `TryGet` / `Remove` (O(1)) / `Find` (O(n) value-search) / `GetAtIndex` (binary-search-from-nearest-end optimization) / `First` / `Count` / `GetEnumerator`.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\LobbyFactory.cs` (~74 LOC — factory keyed by `KeyValuePair<string LobbyName, AppLobbyType>`; `defaultLobby` singleton for empty name; lock-protected dict. `GetOrCreateAppLobby(name, type, out lobby)` lazy-creates. `OnGameServerRemoved(peer)` cascades to default + all lobbies. **Keying hypothesis**: LobbyName likely encodes language/region/tournament-id; type selects backend. Not keyed by pond/tournament/club/FT — those are **game properties**.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\PeerState.cs` (~49 LOC — immutable snapshot `(UserId, UtcCreated)`; discards `PeerBase` ref to allow GC of disconnected peers — native socket-server objects otherwise keep peer reachable and leak. Used in `GameState.joiningPeers`.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\IGameList.cs` (~47 LOC — interface: `Count` / `Games: List<GameState>` (returns null in SqlGameList) / `AddGameState` / `RemoveGameState` / `TryGetGame` / `TryGetRandomGame` / `UpdateGameState` / `CheckJoinTimeOuts` / `AddSubscription` / `PublishGameChanges` / `OnMaxPlayerReached` / `OnPlayerCountFallBelowMaxPlayer` / `RemoveGameServer`. Three impls: `GameList` (in-memory load-aware), `SqlGameList` (SQL-query), `GameChannelList` (property-scoped channels).)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\ILobbyPeer.cs` (~27 LOC — interface: `NetworkProtocol` / `LocalIPAddress` / `LocalPort` / `UserId` / `UseHostnames`. Implemented by `MasterClientPeer`.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\IGameListSubscibtion.cs` (~19 LOC — filename typo `Subscibtion`, preserved; interface: `GetGameList(): Hashtable` + `Dispose()`. Three inner-class impls across backends.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\Lobby\AppLobbyType.cs` (~10 LOC — enum: `Default=0` / `ChannelLobby=1` / `SqlLobby=2`; selects `IGameList` backend in `AppLobby` constructor)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\ChannelLobby\GameChannel.cs` (~353 LOC — per-property-filter game container, lazy-instantiated by `GameChannelList` on first subscription. `key: GameChannelKey` (property hash), `gameDict: LinkedListDictionary` of matching games, `subscriptions: Dictionary<int maxGameCount, HashSet<PeerBase>>` — peers grouped by page-size preference. **Filtering**: a game is included iff all properties in channel.key are present in game.Properties with equal values (`IsSubsetOf`). `OnGameUpdated(state)` adds/removes based on match. `PublishGameChanges` (~39 LOC) iterates per-maxCount subscription buckets, builds + broadcasts `GameListUpdateEvent`. `GetChangedGames(maxCount)` / `GetGameList(maxCount)`. **Auto-cleanup**: inner `Subscription.Dispose` removes peer; when subscription bucket empty removes from subscriptions dict; when subscriptions dict empty, `GameChannelList` removes the channel — cascading GC.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\ChannelLobby\GameChannelList.cs` (~322 LOC — `IGameList` impl delegating to `GameChannel` per-filter. `GameDict: Dictionary<string, GameState>` shared across channels; `GameChannels: Dictionary<GameChannelKey, GameChannel>` lazy-populated. `UpdateGameState` notifies all channels via `OnGameUpdated/OnGameRemoved`. `AddSubscription(peer, filter, maxCount)` creates `GameChannelKey` from filter Hashtable + gets/creates `GameChannel` + adds peer subscription. **`TryGetRandomGame` (~21 LOC) is weaker than `GameList`**: ignores `JoinRandomType` + `query`, linear scan, no LoadLevel sort — just returns first joinable. Likely acceptable for lightweight property-scoped matching.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\MasterServer\ChannelLobby\GameChannelKey.cs` (~31 LOC — `IEquatable<GameChannelKey>` wrapping Hashtable with pre-computed `hashcode` + `DictionaryExtensions.Equals` for value-equality. Enables `GameChannelList.GameChannels` dict keying by property-filter equivalence.)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\Game.cs` (~42 KB — **primary home; the Room class itself**, `class Game : LiteGame, IFishingTogetherPeer.IRoom`). Identity props `PondId` / `TournamentId` / `ClubId` / `FishingTogetherSessionId` + lifecycle props (`isOpen`/`isVisible`/`maxPlayers`/`lobbyId`/`lobbyType`/`isInitializedOnCreate`/`isEnabled`/`goingOffline`/`shouldRemove`). - `fish-registry` — public fish info that players see (names, taxonomy, brief metadata). Does NOT cover closed info (weight ranges, species, spawn locations — that's `fish-generator` and related). Fish is the main character of the game; expect several fish-related modules.

- `ads` — shows in-game ads. Multiple ad types (TargetedAd, WelcomeScreen, PersonalOffer, Unknown) with different lifecycles. 4 partial-class files (~3663 LOC). Core subsystems: (1) event trigger — 40+ game events trigger ad evaluation; (2) condition framework — 50+ condition types (demography / progression / economy / activity / achievements / missions / competitions / fishing / platforms / ad-chains / location) combined with AND-logic + per-condition Negative flag; (3) personal-offers state machine — chain-based offers with Init → Active → ChainElementCooldown → ChainEndCooldown → Expired → respawn, per-design timeouts and cooldowns, concurrent active-offer limit; (4) delivery pipeline — 3-stage filter (Raise → Check conditions → Apply limits), payer/non-payer bucketing, duplicate product prevention, A/B gating, rotation penalty, client notifications. Part of `monetization` system. Also includes payer/cohort targeting (from StatsManager).
  - `WebAdmin\WebAdmin\Models\TargetedAdsStats\` (ad-campaign targeting stats view models)
  - `WebAdmin\WebAdmin\Components\TargetedAdsPlanningTool\` (~16 MB **Vue SPA embedded in Razor** — Vue 2.6.11 + Vuetify 2.2.11 + TS 3.9.3; config-planning UI for PersonalOffers + TargetedAds + WelcomeAds; static reference dictionaries for AchievementStages/Currency/Fish/InventoryItems/Levels/Missions/Ponds/Tournaments)

  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\TargetedAdsManager_ReceiveEvent.cs` (game-event triggers + condition framework — `CheckAdConditions`, `CheckConditions`, `CheckCondition`, `CheckAbTestCondition`, `CheckDisplayCondition`, `CheckDesignConditions`; 50+ condition-type switch in `InternalCheckConditionBeforeNegation` — 339 LOC)

- `reel-of-fortune` — gives a random prize; two variants: regular (free) and golden (premium) spins with distinct analytics streams (`LogReelOfFortuneFact` vs `LogReelOfFortuneGoldFact`) and distinct `BalanceMovementType.{Regular/Golden}ReelOfFortuneReward`. Part of `monetization` system. **Cross-trigger**: third-party ads can grant additional spins (`ReceiveAdditionalSpinsForAd`).
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Fortune\` (12 files ~963 LOC — ReelOfFortuneContext (ITrackable) + ReelOfFortuneEventType + Reward + GoldenReelContext)

  - `Dal\Sql.MsSql\Fortune\SqlReelOfFortuneProvider.cs` (~29 LOC impl; sproc wrapper)

ops: `Init` (attempts golden-reel activation) / `CheckForDailyReel` (new-day UTC check + counter increment) / `PerformSpin(spinType)` (validates state + RNG-picks reward + applies via peer) / `PerformGoldenSpin` (premium-currency cost + golden-rewards + logs spin cost) / `ReceiveAdditionalSpinsForAd` (third-party ad integration); event-subscriptions `Profile.ProductAdded` (Premium/StarterKit bonus spins) + `OnBalanceChange` (golden reel trigger) + `SubscriptionEnded` (remove spins); `Execute` wrapper inits rewards/golden-rewards from cache + validates state + flushes context post-op. `ReelOfFortuneAdapter_Peristence.cs` (**filename typo — should be `_Persistence`**, ~63 LOC partial — duplicate `BulkLoadFirstProductInRewards` / `BulkLoadItemInRewards` static helpers; platform-aware product filtering via `PlatformMapping.SupportedPlatformIds`). `ReelOfFortuneAdapterExtensions.cs` (~98 LOC — DTO mappers for `ReelOfFortuneCohort(CohortId/MinLevel/MaxLevel)` / `ReelOfFortuneReward.FromDtoSafe/NoSafe` (parses products JSON, throws on `throwException=true`) / `ReelOfFortuneGoldDay` / `ReelOfFortuneGoldReward` items+products / `ReelOfFortuneGoldSpinPrice(SpinId/SpinNumber/Currency/Amount)`; `GiveReelOfFortuneReward` private helper increments profile balance).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Fortune.cs` (~6 KB, `IReelOfFortunePeer` impl): `ReelOfFortuneAdapter` lazy init (wires peer + `DalFactory.GetLogger().Fortune`); `ShowDailyReel` / `ActivateGoldenReel` (4 LOC each — client events `OnDailyReel` / `OnGoldenReelActivated`); **`FlushContextChangesToClient` (15 LOC)** — tracker delta serialization + `LoadRewardViewData(Profile.LanguageId)` preload of golden-reward item details before `OnContextChanged` event; `GiveRegularReelOfFortuneReward` / `GiveGoldenReelOfFortuneReward` delegate to `GiveReelOfFortuneReward(reward, BalanceMovementType)` → `RewardManager.ProcessReward`; `PublishBalanceChangesToClient` → `NotifyClientAboutBalanceChange`; **`HandleReelOfFortuneOperation` (50 LOC)** — 3-op dispatcher: `PerformSpin` (parses `ReelOfFortuneSpinType`), `PerformGoldenSpin`, `ReceiveAdditionalSpinsForAd` (**`#if DEBUG` only** — dev backdoor)

- `third-party-ads` — **DEPRECATED module** (server code still present and partially functional, but **client-side SDKs have been removed** — the feature is effectively dead). External ad-network integration (AdMob / Unity Ads / etc.) — **distinct from `ads` (TargetedAds)**. Lifecycle: generate → show → satisfy | invalidate; show-limit window enforced via `GlobalVariablesCache.ThirdPartyAdsShowLimitExpiration`. Historically triggered from many game events (DailyReward / EndOfDay / TimeForwardCooldownRemoval). Was part of `monetization` system (ad-revenue). **Candidate for removal** after audit of remaining server-side callers.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\ThirdPartyAdsAdapter.cs` (ad-lifecycle manager with UnitOfWork pattern — Mongo logging integration): `GenerateAd` filter by active/premium/conditions + pick one + check show-limit (1/day) + log fact; `ShowAd` check show-limit + increment history counter + log fact; `SatisfyAd` execute reward (currency / reel-of-fortune spins / time-forward-skip); `InvalidateAd` timeout/user-cancel path. **Client SDKs removed; server code is stub-only for compat.**
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\IThirdPartyAdsPeer.cs` (interface contract for ad-reward delivery + condition checking — premium + level constraints)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\MockThirdPartyAdsPeer.cs` (test double with level-condition validation)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_ThirdPartyAds.cs` (~9 KB, `IThirdPartyAdsPeer` impl): `ThirdPartyAdsAdapter` lazy init (applies `ShowLimitExpiration` from global config); **`TriggerThirdPartyAd(string, Reward, Dictionary)` (26 LOC)** — public entry: generate ad → execute → capture state changes → send event or add to params (called from many game-event sites — cross-module leak candidates); interface impls: `CheckConditions` → `TargetedAdsManager.CheckConditions` (cross-link to `ads`), `RemoveTimeForwardCooldown` → `Profile.MoveTimeForwardTimeout=null` + Travel logger (leak into `time-mechanics`), `GiveThirdPartyReward` → `RewardManager.SelectSpecificReward/ProcessReward` with `BalanceMovementType.ThirdPartyAd`, `ReceiveAdditionalSpinsForAd` → `ReelOfFortuneAdapter.ReceiveAdditionalSpinsForAd` (cross-link to `reel-of-fortune`), `LogThirdPartyAdFact` → analytics; `UnloadThirdPartyAds` (11 LOC — shutdown + state-changes capture + `OnUnloaded` event); **`HandleThirdPartyAdsOperation` (99 LOC god-dispatcher, 6 sub-ops)**: `GenerateAd` / `GenerateAdByCategory` / `GenerateMultipleAds` (comma-split names — see section N) / `ShowAd` / `SatisfyAd` / `InvalidateAd`

**`UnitOfWork_IncomingItemReceived.cs` (~203 LOC gift-push handler)** — checks not-yet-pushed + `ProcessPushAt` window + user-has-devices + inactivity ≥ 15 min default, parses gift JSON via SerializationHelper, inner SendSkipper skips online; - ~~`ranks`~~ — **merged into `levels`**. Rank progression after level cap lives in the same `LevelingManager.IncrementExperience` flow. Analytics touchpoint `LogRankEarned` stays in AnalyticsAdapter and is reached from the same path.
- `time-mechanics` — game-time model: 1:4 real-to-game ratio (1 real hour = 4 in-game hours; 1 in-game minute = 15 real seconds). Supports fast-forward to skip no-bite periods (with cooldown + paid removal). Weather (and therefore bite) are tied to game time. Day-end detection, pond-stay timing, level-lock forced exits.
  - `Shared\DT\Helper.cs`
  - `Shared\Photon.Interfaces\SharedMethods\InGameTimeHelper.cs` + `TimeRewinder.cs` (~136 LOC — **misplaced** in Photon.Interfaces but namespace says `SharedLib.Game`): `InGameTimeHelper` (pond-day calc ≠ calendar-day, starts at 5am, max 30-day stays, `IsNewDayStarted`, `HasPondStayFinished`); `TimeRewinder` (cooldown multiplier removing night hours from time-forward cost). Consumed by game-state + fishing-session (**cross-cutting infra primitive** used as `DT.Helper.UtcNow` everywhere): swappable UTC provider via injectable `Now` delegate (test-time override); FP standard format `yyyy/MM/dd HH:mm:ss` parse/format + Unix-time helpers. No external I/O — pure in-memory. **Mutable static `Now` delegate is not thread-safe** (concurrent `Reset` races); mitigated by test-only use.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Travel.cs` (**`HandleTimeOperation`** (**306 LOC god-method**): GetTime / MoveTimeForward / GetTimeForwardCooldown / RemoveTimeForwardCooldown; `UpdateProfileTimeToCurrent` (91 LOC — tournament/league sync, multipliers, FTG sync, day-end, level-lock), `TryFinalizeDay` (77 LOC), `ProcessDayChange`, `DebugMoveTimeForward`, `HandleGetServerTimeRequest`)
  - (analytics touchpoints in AnalyticsAdapter: `LogMoveTimeForward`, `LogRemoveTimeForwardCooldown`)
- `buoys` — players place buoys on the pond to mark spots (good bite locations, nav waypoints, etc.). Covers full lifecycle: placement / take / rename / share (via ChatServer) / accept-shared / decline-shared / recolor (free allowance per pond → premium ratio → paid GC) + navigation-buoy fast-travel + pinned-location tracking + cooldown removal. Absorbs what was previously a separate `navigation` module — navigation-buoys are just one type of buoy.

- `competitive` **(system)** — umbrella for player-vs-player scored activities. Contains 3 activity kinds (each with its own lifecycle) plus 2 shared engines. Code uses the name "tournament" throughout (`TournamentAdapter`, `TournamentsCache`, `TournamentProvider`, `TournamentKinds` enum) because tournaments came first; scoring/results code is shared by all 3 kinds.

- `tournament-scoring` — **shared** scoring engine used by tournaments + competitions + user-generated. Validates fish (species, weight, length, rod match, equipment restrictions, origin), computes primary + secondary scores (18 `TournamentScoreType` variants), manages fish eviction (FishCount limit), marks scoring fish. Also hosts the rating-delta engine + bracket-seeding engine for competitions. Part of `competitive` system. Name keeps "tournament-" prefix because code does.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Tournaments\TournamentRatingCalculator.cs` (~140 LOC — deterministic rating-delta calculation; 5 skill buckets (Noob 0-99 / Amateur 100-1199 / SemiPro 1200-1999 / Pro 2000-2499 / Elite 2500+) with ZeroPoint / MaxWin / MaxLoose interpolated by bucket; zPoint = `Interpolate(zPointMultiplier * (participantCount-3) + 3)`; win-formula + loose-formula with place-modifier taper (1.0/0.9/0.8/0.75…). `IsRatingByPlaceEnabled` alternative checked in `ProcessTournamentResult` on game-server. **Dual-implementation concern** — `TournamentsHelper.CalculateTournamentRatingGained` is a parallel entry point)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Tournaments\MatchmakingLogic.cs` (~821 LOC — **tournament-bracket seeding engine** — NOT room-matchmaking (per user rule); distributes competition participants into groups/brackets by skill rating). Entry `ProcessGrouping(TournamentDto, provider)` + `ProcessGroupingForTournament(Tournament)`. 3-phase algorithm: (1) `CreateBuckets` partitions by bracket rating-range; (2) `BalanceBuckets` 109 LOC ping-pong traversal moves players between adjacent buckets to meet MinSize; (3) `BuildGroups` per-bucket or FFS global allocation. **FFS (Free-Fill-Swap) algorithm 240 LOC** — when `MaxGroupCount` set: phase 1 maximize groups, phase 2 reduce to budget, phase 3 rebalance toward `TargetSize` via Free/Fill/Swap operations using `Rational` struct for exact arithmetic (avoids float-loss). No-split rule for lowest bracket (MinRating=0). Excel-style group naming (A/B/…/Z/AA/AB…). Convergence capped at 100 iterations.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\DalAdapters\TournamentAdapter.cs` (methods: `CaptureFish`, `CaptureFishCatchInt`, `PreviewFishTake`, `UpdateOverallTournamentScore`, `RemoveFishFromCage`, `GetScore` (god method, 188 LOC), `UpdateStats` (2 overloads), `EnsureStats`, `MarkScoringFish`, `PostUpdateStats`, `PostUpdateSecondaryStats`, `LogFishExclusionReason`)
- `tournament-results` — **shared** results / leaderboards / notifications used by tournaments + competitions + user-generated. Saves individual + team results, computes player/team place, notifies client about tournament updates and final results, exports secondary-result leaderboard + history. Part of `competitive` system.

  - `Shared\SharedLib\Profile\UserAccountAdapter.cs` (~220 LOC — **multi-account binding logic**, consumed by `ProfileAdapter.RegisterUser` (3 call-sites) + `ProfileAdapter.GetAllUserAccounts` + `MasterAuthenticator.cs` + `WebAdmin\PlayerController.cs`): `GetAllUserAccounts(source, externalId)` retrieves accounts linked by shared external ID; `GenerateUsername` / `GenerateUsernameUnique(maxRetries)` from `UsernamePartsCache` + numeric suffixes (**infinite-loop risk if cache empty**); `DeleteUserAccount(userId, isDeleted)` soft-delete with cascading activation of sibling account; `ActivateUserAccount(userId)` switches active + deactivates previous. Uses `new Random(Guid.NewGuid().GetHashCode())` per-instance — **weak entropy under concurrent init**.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Profile\AccountBindingHelper.cs` (~111 LOC — **multi-platform account binding**): `GetAssociatedAccounts(userId)` retrieves accounts linked by historical ExternalId; `UnbindPlayerFromPlatformSaveReference(userId)` deactivate + unlink; `RebindPlayerToPlatform(userId)` reactivate + restore; `PlayerCanBeRebound(userId)` check. Consumed by `ProfileAdapter.DeleteUserAccount` (~L2106 if immediate-unbind-enabled).

- `end-of-day` — pond-session conclusion; the single most coupled operation in the codebase. `SendEndOfDayResult` is ~210 LOC across 9 phases (day-validity + cage inspection → fish sell → daily wear → period stats → rent expiry → 3rd-party ad trigger → analytics & event broadcast → missions hook → bite-system reseed). Also handles mission-result variant. Touches ~15 modules. Name is provisional — expand / split later as the rest of the codebase comes into focus.

  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Friendship.cs` (~332 LOC — client-peer side; **S2S chat-server messaging-based lifecycle**. `SendFriendshipMessage` (2 overloads — string/char message; `isOffline=true` + `expiration=DT.Helper.UtcNow.AddDays(MessageLifetime.FriendshipRequest)`); **`OnSendMessage_Friendship` (49 LOC)** outbound filter — 6 branches over ChatMessage: `AddToFriends` request / `RemoveFromFriends` / `RemoveFromFriendsAndIgnore` / `Answer+PositiveAnswer` (accept) / `Answer+NegativeAnswer` (decline) / `Answer+IgnoreAnswer` (rewrites outbound to NegativeAnswer); **`OnReceiveMessage_Friendship` (78 LOC god — inbound S2S dispatcher)** — 6 branches: `AddToFriends` inbound (max-100 guard via `GlobalVariablesCache.MaxFriendsCount` → auto-reject with `SendFriendshipMessage` if capped + DAL log; else `AddFriend(FriendshipRequest)` + `SerializationHelper.SerializeFriend(AddToFriends, friend)` into messageEvent.Data), `RemoveFromFriends` / `RemoveFromFriendsAndIgnore`, `Unignored` (→ `RemoveFriend(onlyIfNotIgnored:true, addToUnfriended:false)`), `PositiveAnswer` (→ `AddFriend(Friend)`), `NegativeAnswer` (→ `RemoveFriend`); core lifecycle: **`AddFriend` (52 LOC)** — add or promote (FriendshipRequested → FriendshipRequest → Friend); max-100 guard + self-account check + status-transition rules + RequestTime tracking, delegates to `ProfileAdapter.GetFriend(Guid)`; **`RemoveFriend` (36 LOC)** — optional `onlyIfNotIgnored` / `addToUnfriended`; leak to `buoys` via `Profile.RemoveBuoyShareRequestsOfPlayer(Guid)`; **`IgnoreFriend` (27 LOC)** — set to Ignore, clear RequestTime, clean `Profile.FriendsUnfriended` list, remove buoy-share requests; **`UnignoreFriend` (19 LOC)** — send `Unignored` message via `SendFriendshipMessage`; **`AddNewFriend` (24 LOC)** — `ProfileAdapter.GetFriend(Guid)` + self-account guard (`Profile.Source + ExternalId`) + unfriended list management. Cross-module leaks: `buoys` (`RemoveBuoyShareRequestsOfPlayer`), `messaging` (chat-server S2S), `account-lifecycle` (self-account detection via Source + ExternalId))
- `rewards` — reward lookup + processing + claim flow (with source: CompetitiveLeaderboard / GlobalLeaderboard / FishLeaderboard / DailyBonus / …). Includes: deferred rewards (queued on profile, claimed later), immediate reward processing (exp + money + ext + items + products + licenses + skin elements), loot-table selection, daily-bonus scheduling (per-platform: `Day1-5` vs `PSDay1-5` for PlayStation). Coupled with `product-delivery` (via `ProductDeliveryService`), `reel-of-fortune` (daily-bonus blocked if RoF active), `ads` (DailyReward third-party ad trigger), `levels`/`achievements`/`inventory-items`/`licenses`.
