Constants `BaseCurrency="USD"`, `BaseCountry="--"`.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Monetization\LocalPriceCalculator.cs` (~285 LOC — **Smart Beautify regional price-beautification algorithm**): 3-tier snap-to-grid (Gold coarse 10/1000× min-unit → Silver medium 1/100× → Bronze fine 0.1/10×) with ±3% deviation guard. Tiered preference Gold > Silver > Bronze, but Gold only chosen if extra cost ≤ threshold (0.5% for raw-price < 100; 1.5% otherwise). Fallback cascade beauty → grid-fallback (if min-unit ≥ 1 & ±5% dev) → bronze directional. Rate ≥ 1 (premium) → prefer up-rounding; rate < 1 (discount) → prefer down-rounding. Legacy `[Obsolete]` `CalculateRegionalPrice` overload kept for GD validation — scheduled for removal.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\CurrencyExchange\` (6 files ~113 LOC — **CurrencyFreaks.com external API integration** for USD-equivalent revenue calc): `CurrencyExchangeExtensions.cs` DI registration → singleton `CurrencyFreaksRateDownloader`; `IRateDownloader.cs` contract `GetExchangeRates() → IDictionary<string, decimal>`; `CurrencyFreaks\CurrencyFreaksRateDownloader.cs` lazy-load HTTP client to `https://api.currencyfreaks.com/v2.0/` (fetches supported currencies → `rates/latest?base=USD&symbols=...&apikey=...`); 3 DTOs (`GetLatestRatesResponse` / `GetSupportedCountriesResponse` / `SupportedCurrency` filters "Crypto"). Feeds `MonetizationCache.GetCurrencyExchangeRate` consumed by `MonetizationHelper.TryGetEquivalentPrice`. **Single API-key in app.config — silent-failure if empty**: all `GetExchangeRates` return empty dict → USD revenue calc falls back to raw local amount.

  - `Shared\Twitch\TwitchApiUtils.cs` (Twitch Helix API helper — modern `HttpClient` based; static facade): `ValidateToken` (`id.twitch.tv/oauth2/validate`), `RefreshToken` async via OAuth token endpoint, `GetDropEntitlements` paginated iterator for unfulfilled drops, `FulfillDropEntitlements` batch-PATCH mark-fulfilled. DTOs: `TokenValidationInfo`/`TokenInfo`/`DropEntitlement`/`TwitchApiErrorResponse`. Separate from `Twitch\TwitchAccountLinking\` OAuth service (account-binding, top-level folder).
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\Monetization\TwitchManager.cs` (single method: `DeliverDrops(peer)`)
- `twitch-account-linking` — **standalone ASP.NET Core MVC service** that lets players link their Twitch account to their FP account (prerequisite for Twitch Drops). OAuth2 auth-code flow for Twitch + platform-specific auth via `oauth-providers` sub-modules (Steam/PS/Apple/Google/Epic/Xbox/Nintendo). Separate deployment from main game-server.
  - `Twitch\TwitchAccountLinking\` (15 .cs + 5 views): `Program.cs` host-builder; `Startup.cs` auth-middleware chain (Steam OpenID + OAuth providers + cookie auth + session, 10-day timeout); `Controllers\AuthenticationController.cs` provider-selection + redirect; `Controllers\HomeController.cs` link/unlink lifecycle (OIDC state validation + Twitch token exchange + DB link persistence); `DAL\DalAdapter.cs` DB link-table writes; `Utils\TwitchApiClient.cs` Twitch token+user endpoint calls; `Utils\SteamApiUtils.cs` Steam user-ID extraction; models `SignInConfigurationModel`/`ErrorViewModel`/`SupportedPlatforms`/`UserInfo`/`TwitchLoginResultModel`; views SignIn/Index/Unlink + shared layout.
- `oauth-providers` — **umbrella module** (per L section recommendation) wrapping 4 platform OAuth handlers, each an ASP.NET Core library extending `OAuthHandler<T>` for community-style registration via `.Add[Platform](options => {...})`. Consumed by `twitch-account-linking` + any future service needing platform OAuth.
  - `Twitch\AspNet.Security.OAuth.Epic\` (5 files — `EpicAuthenticationHandler` JWT introspection via `IdentityModel.TokenIntrospectionRequest` + Options/Defaults/Extensions registration helper)
  - `Twitch\AspNet.Security.OAuth.Nintendo\` (4 files — minimal: Options + Defaults + Extensions; handler missing/inherited)
  - `Twitch\AspNet.Security.OAuth.PlayStation\` (6 files — handler with Basic-auth header from `ClientId:ClientSecret` + PlayStationAuthenticationInitializer pre-auth config + external-logout URI; Scope/Defaults/Constants/Options)
  - `Twitch\AspNet.Security.OAuth.XBox\` (6 files — handler with form-body `client_secret` + `AuthUserRequest`/`AuthUserResponse` DTOs + Options/Extensions)
- `webhooks` — **standalone ASP.NET Core API service** receiving events from external systems (primarily Denuvo anti-cheat; extensible). API-versioned (V1 + V2). Validates via `X-FP-API-Key` header middleware; logs ban events to MongoDB; disconnect-signal to online users if banned in real-time.
  - `WebServices\WebHooks\WebHooks\` (25 files): `Program.cs` host-builder (API versioning + Swagger + API-key middleware); **`Controllers\V1,V2\AnticheatController.cs`** — 2 webhook endpoints `GET /api/v{version}/anticheat/denuvo/label/cheater/{externalId}` + `label/vac-banned/{externalId}`; flow: platform→externalId resolution → user-brief fetch (main+stats SQL) → Denuvo label validation (env `ImmediateBanOn` + `NonPayersOnlyBan` with **payable-exemption** logic) → ban decision → user-ban + disconnect-signal (if online) → MongoDB log `DenuvoBan`; `DAL\DalAdapter.cs` SQL/Mongo connection pooling + ban/user ops (**legacy `System.Data.SqlClient` direct `SqlCommand` strings — not parameterized EF/Dapper**); `DAL\MongoDB\` MongoAccessor + BanLog + MongoLog + OnlineCache; `Helpers\PlatformHelper.cs` platform detection; `Middleware\ApiKeyAuthentication.cs` header validation; `ObjectModel\Denuvo\` (DenuvoBan/DenuvoLabel/config) + `UserBrief`/`OnlineSession`/`ServerInstallation`/`PlatformSources`; `Swagger\ConfigureSwaggerOptions.cs` OpenAPI setup. **TODO comment re: ban-source refactor** — known debt.
- `software-distributor` — **standalone ASP.NET MVC 4.0 (.NET Framework 4.7.2, deprecated/EOL 2026) UI** for server-farm lifecycle management. Ops can start/stop nodes, download/apply updates, manage peer nodes, monitor status via AJAX. Already flagged in F section as "active — can start/stop servers, install updates". Uses SimpleMembership (pre-Identity) for auth.
  - `SoftwareDistributor\SoftwareDistributor\` (21 files): `Global.asax.cs` ASP.NET MVC app lifecycle; **`Controllers\HomeController.cs`** — farm/node management (`Index` AJAX dashboard + `GetStatus/{nodeId}` + `DownloadUpdate(farmName)` broadcasts `CommandDownload` + `StartAll`/`StopAll`/`ApplyUpdate` lifecycle + `Add(nodeId)`/`Remove(nodeId)` peer mgmt); `AccountController` + `ManageController` boilerplate; `Settings.cs` app-config (NodeRole + directories + service names Photon/AsyncService); `SoftwareDistribution\ScriptExecutor.cs` remote script invocation on nodes; `App_Start\*` + `Filters\InitializeSimpleMembershipAttribute.cs` legacy auth.
  - `SoftwareDistributor\DistributorCommon\` (shared library): **`Distributor.cs` singleton** loads `Distributor.json` config (farms + nodes) and broadcasts commands; `Farm.cs` (node collection); `Node.cs` (role RoleDist/RoleGame + status + version installed/downloaded + load + peer count); `Enums.cs` (RoleDist/RoleGame + command types Start/Stop/Download/Apply/Add/Remove). **Synchronous I/O in constructor** — `.Result` on file load blocks on network-FS.
  - `SoftwareDistributor\Actions\GameCarrier\` + `Configs\GameCarrier\` — GameCarrier-specific automation + config (installed/downloaded version tracking).
- `fishing-session` — per-pond fishing activity session: when player arrives at a pond, a regular fishing session starts and fish caught go into the fish cage until end-of-day. If the player switches to a tournament / fishing-together, the regular session is saved and a custom session is started; restored on return. Saves each catch with metadata (cycle, fish, equipment, fight duration) via `IFishingSessionProvider`. Candidate for merging with `game-session` later — tentative.
  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Stats\IFishingSessionProvider.cs` (per-pond session persistence contract)
  - `Dal\Sql.MsSql\Stats\SqlFishStatsProvider.cs` (~592 LOC impl) + `SqlPlayerStatsProvider.cs` (~76 LOC) + `SqlLeagueStatsProvider.cs` (~25 LOC); TOP 1 placements, MIN/MAX/GROUP BY without explicit sort guarantees
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\FishingSessionManager.cs`
- `tablet` — in-game tablet feature: gates which screens/tools the player can see on the pond (boat screen, echo sounder, fish radar), computes isobar step for the map display. Depends on boat equipment (EchoSounder with GPS + IsobarStep/IsobarDet, FishRadar) and mission completion. Special rules for rent-boats on Okinawa (Japan).
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Radar\IMapSettingsProvider.cs` (~29 LOC interface: `CurrentSettings` (`TabletMapSettings`) + `Refresh()` bool-on-change + `MockMapSettingsProvider` singleton; impl in GameLogic's `MapSettingsProvider` — game-server side already catalogued)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\MapSettingsProvider.cs` (implements `IMapSettingsProvider`; constants `MaxSaltwaterIsobarCount=40`, `MaxFreshwaterIsobarCount=20`)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_TabletMap.cs` (tiny 38 LOC): `MapSettingsProvider` lazy property (6 LOC, takes profile + errorLogging); `RefreshMapSettings` (14 LOC — checks if refresh needed, broadcasts `TabletMapSettingsUpdated` event to client + FT host via `FishingTogetherAdapter.RefreshTabletMapSettings` if IsHost)
- `fish-radar` — shows fish on the map (via boat-mounted radar or tablet). Gate managed by `tablet` module; actual radar data generation lives in `Shared\SharedLib\Radar\`.
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Radar\` (5 files ~373 LOC: FishRadarContext + LocationFishData + SquareLocation + FishRadarDataChangeSet)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Radar\FishRadarManager.cs` (~350 LOC — **the main class** already referenced as lazy-init on `GameClientPeer_Radar`): depends on `IFishRadarHost` (boat context) + `FishRadarContext` (caching); `EnsureStarted()` lazy-init + schedule refresh; `RefreshFishRadarData()` main loop; **`GetLocations()` BFS** over reachable grid-squares given boat movement constraints; uses `RadarAreaPrediction` to calculate max-travel-distance + visibility; caches `LocationFishData` (bite probability per grid-square) with 4-min refresh interval; logs changes as `FishRadarDataChangeSet` + notifies host via `OnUpdateReady`. Consumes `GameServerCache.GetPondConfiguration`, `host.BiteMap` (bite-system dep), `GlobalVariablesCache.SonarSquareLength`.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Radar\IFishRadarHost.cs` (~43 LOC interface — **impl'd by `GameClientPeer_Radar`**): `BiteMap`/`PlayerBiteData`/`WeatherName`/`WindDirection`/`StayTimeMinutes`/`Position Point3`/`Rotation`/`MaxSpeed`/`CurrentSpeed`/`PondId`/`DetailedLogging` props; `ShouldGenerateRadarData(out reason)` + `GetFishRadar()` + `ScheduleRefresh(action, interval)` + `OnUpdateReady(context)` + `Log`/`LogException`.
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Radar\RadarAreaPrediction.cs` (~100 LOC static utility): `GetMaxReachableDistance(boatSpeed, maxSpeed, maxAcceleration, timeLimitSeconds)` calculates boat travel distance with acceleration curve; `IsInArea(testLocation, radarRange, boatPosition, boatRotation, maxSailDistance)` visibility check with 1.2× backward-area multiplier; private `IsBehind()` rotation-matrix math.
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_Radar.cs` (217 LOC client-facing + IFishRadarHost implementation): `HandleGetSounderFish` (24 LOC — feature-flag `GlobalVariablesCache.ReplaceSonarDataWithFishRadar` switches between new `FishRadarManager.GetFishDataAtPointAndNearby` and legacy `processor.GetSounderFish`); `TransformToSonarData` (25 LOC — radar `LocationFishData` → 6-float sonar array for top/mid/bottom layers); `FishSizeToKilograms` enum map (Large=5 / Medium=3 / Small=1 kg); `IsOnOwnBoat` (boat not rent); lazy `FishRadarManager` property (context routes FT-room OR null); **`IFishRadarHost` interface impl (~130 LOC)**: `BiteMap`/`PlayerBiteData` (to Processor.BiteMap + commented `MockPondBiteData`), `Weather`/`Wind`/`PondId`/`Position`/`Rotation`/`MaxSpeed`/`CurrentSpeed` properties (to Processor.Config + BoatManager); `ShouldGenerateRadarData` (45 LOC guard god-method: finalized / !boarded / FTG capability `Saltwater Radar` / physics-host / game-paused / boat-has-radar); `GetFishRadar` (extract FishRadar item from boat nested items); `ScheduleRefresh`/`OnUpdateReady`/`SendFishRadarUpdatedEvent` (compress + send delta); `Log/LogException/DetailedLogging` stubs)
- `skins` — cosmetic-customization module: skin elements (emblems / colors / logos) organized by type / sub-type / content-type; consumed by `clubs` `_Logo` subsystem for club logos AND premium-character customization. `SkinsCache` is L0-tier; `SkinElementPrice` pricing model lives in `Shared\SharedLib\Clubs\`.
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Skins\` (5 files ~67 LOC: SkinElement + SkinElementType + SkinContentType + SkinSubType)
  - `Shared\Photon.Interfaces\SkinElements\` (3 files ~20 LOC minimal: SkinElementsSubOperationCode `GetAll=0` only + ParameterCode + ErrorCode — single read-only op, absorbed into `clubs` club-logo editor)
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\Inventory\Outfit\` (3 files ~42 LOC — avatar clothing enums)
  - `Dal\Sql.Interface\Skins\` (~5 files ~81 LOC — `ISkinsProvider`: `GetAllSkinElements` / `GetAllSkinElementTypes` / `GetAllSkinSubTypes` / `GetAllSkinContentType`; DTOs `SkinElementDto` / `SkinElementTypeDto` / `SkinSubTypeDto` / `SkinContentTypeDto`)
  - `Dal\Sql.MsSql\Skins\SkinsProvider.cs` (~20 LOC impl — **inherits `ProviderBase` directly, NOT `SqlProviderBase`** — inheritance mismatch with siblings; class name lacks `Sql` prefix)
  - `Shared\SharedLib\Clubs\SkinElementPrice.cs` + `SkinHelper.cs` (pricing + logging — already catalogued under `clubs` module; shared here for completeness)
- `rate-us` — App Store / Play Store rating popup with pre-popup warm-up dialog flow: platform gate (RateUsSupportedPlatforms), level gate (RateUsPopupShowLevel), warm-up limit (RateUsMaxWarmUpDialogShowTimes), inter-show delay (RateUsPopupDelayHours), debouncing (1s). Registers user's warm-up answers (up to 20 stored).
  - `Shared\ObjectModel\RateUs\` (3 files ~76 LOC: RateUsPopupStatus + RateUsWarmUpDialogAnswer + RateUsWarmUpDialogButtonType)
  - `Shared\Photon.Interfaces\RateUs\RateUsSubOperationCode.cs` (1 file 8 LOC: RegisterWarmUpDialogAnswer + RegisterPopupShow)
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameLogic\RateUsManager.cs`
  - `Photon\src-server\Loadbalancing\LoadBalancing\GameServer\GameClientPeer_RateUs.cs` (~54 LOC — thin client-facing partial): `HandleRateUsOperation` (~35 LOC dispatcher, 2 sub-ops): `RegisterWarmUpDialogAnswer` (parses `RateUsWarmUpDialogAnswer` from compressed JSON → `RateUsManager.RegisterWarmUpDialogAnswer` → returns show-count); `RegisterPopupShow` (→ `RateUsManager.RegisterRateUsPopupShow` → returns show-count); default throws `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`
